# <a name="glossary"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-103">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-103">Glossary</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="cc989-104">以下是「Microsoft [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] 說明」中所採用的詞彙及其定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-104">The following terms and definitions are used in Microsoft [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] Help.</span></span>  
  
## <a name=""></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-105">。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-105">.</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-106">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-106">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-107">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-107">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-108">.brl file (.brl 檔)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-108">.brl file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-109">商務規則定義檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-109">A business rules definition file.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-110">.btm file (.btm 檔)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-110">.btm file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-111">BizTalk Server 對應檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-111">A BizTalk Server map file.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-112">.btp file (.btp 檔)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-112">.btp file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-113">BizTalk Server 管線檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-113">A BizTalk Server pipeline file.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-114">.btproj</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-114">.btproj</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-115">BizTalk 專案檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-115">A BizTalk project file.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-116">.btt file (.btt 檔)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-116">.btt file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-117">追蹤設定檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-117">A tracking profile file.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-118">.odx file (.odx 檔)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-118">.odx file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-119">BizTalk Server 協調流程檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-119">A BizTalk Server orchestration file.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-120">.xsd file (.xsd 檔)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-120">.xsd file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-121">BizTalk Server 結構描述檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-121">A BizTalk Server schema file.</span></span>|  
|||  
  
## <a name="a"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-122">A</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-122">A</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-123">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-123">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-124">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-124">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-125">action</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-125">action</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-126">對應到規則 "THEN" 部分的一或多個函數，用來指定條件為真時該執行哪些動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-126">One or more functions corresponding to the "THEN" part of a rule and used to specify what is to be done when a condition evaluates to true.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-127">Activate property (啟動屬性)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-127">Activate property</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-128">「接收」圖形的屬性，用來表示收到訊息時即啟動協調流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-128">A property of the Receive shape, used to indicate that the orchestration is activated when a message is received.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-129">在協調流程中，可標示為啟動的「接收」圖形僅限於第一個傳送或接收的啟動圖形。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-129">The Receive shape can only be marked as activated if it is the first send- or receive-activated shape in an orchestration.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-130">activation block (啟動區塊)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-130">activation block</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-131">活動模型內的一組步驟或動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-131">A grouping of steps or actions within an activity model.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-132">activation receive (啟動接收)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-132">activation receive</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-133">用於簡稱「接收」圖形的啟動屬性設定為 True 的表達方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-133">A shorthand expression for the condition of the Receive shape when the Activate property on this shape is set to True.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-134">activity model (活動模型)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-134">activity model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-135">預先定義的一連串動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-135">A predefined sequence of actions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-136">在啟動區塊中可以叫用這些動作序列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-136">These can be invoked in activation blocks.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-137">activity model step (活動模型步驟)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-137">activity model step</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-138">從活動模型的觀點而言，就是動作的同義字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-138">A synonym for an action from the viewpoint of an activity model.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-139">當動作包含於活動模型內時，就是所謂的活動模型步驟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-139">When an action is contained within an activity model, it is referred to as an activity model step.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-140">activity node (活動節點)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-140">activity node</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-141">包含里程碑和資料項目的節點，這些項目代表商務分析師有興趣的資料，他們透過 Microsoft Excel 精靈建立這些資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-141">A node that contains the milestones and data items that represent the data of interest to the business analyst, which the analyst creates using Microsoft Excel wizards.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-142">activity window (活動視窗)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-142">activity window</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-143">定義活動執行個體資料可見的時間週期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-143">Defines the time period over which activity instance data is visible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-144">這些資料永遠都在變更中，因為時間點永遠都在變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-144">The data is always changing because the point in time is always changing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-145">當透過活動視窗傳遞資料之後，您可以執行資料維護 DTS/SSIS 套件，將資料移到 BAM 封存資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-145">After the data passes through the activity window you can move it to the BAM Archive database by running the Data Maintenance DTS/SSIS package.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-146">當您將資料移到 BAM 封存資料庫之後，就無法再使用這些資料來進行 BAM 入口網站上的查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-146">After you move it to the BAM Archive database, it is no longer available for queries on the BAM portal.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-147">actor (執行者)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-147">actor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-148">開始活動或參與活動的人或程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-148">A person or process that either starts or participates in an activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-149">執行者可以是啟動者或目標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-149">Actors can be either initiators or targets.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-150">adapter (配接器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-150">adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-151">COM 或 .NET 元件，協助在應用程式 (例如商業實務系統) 與 BizTalk Server 之間交換訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-151">A COM or .NET-based component that helps exchange messages between applications (for example, a line-of-business system) and BizTalk Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-152">配協器由設計階段元件和執行階段元件組成，進行接收和傳送的作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-152">The adapter consists of design-time components and run-time components for receive and send operations.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-153">adapter framework (配接器架構)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-153">adapter framework</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-154">建置 BizTalk 配接器的規格，使用以 Web 服務為基礎的開放標準。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-154">The specifications for building BizTalk adapters using open standards based on Web Services.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-155">addendum (增補)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-155">addendum</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-156">協議的一小部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-156">A piece of an agreement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-157">協議是由多個增補所組成，以定義採用的商務程序、您的角色、夥伴的角色、在此關係中使用的原則或參數，以及商務與法律條款等表列文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-157">An agreement consists of multiple addendums that define the business process that is used, your role, your partner’s role, and the policies or parameters that are used in that relationship along with documentation, such as a list of business and legal terms.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-158">affiliate application (分支應用程式)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-158">affiliate application</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-159">企業單一登入 (Single Sign-On，SSO) 中的邏輯實體，由管理員定義，表示主機、後端系統或商業實務應用程式等應用程式的系統或子系統，您透過 SSO 與這些系統進行連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-159">A logical entity in Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO), defined by the administrator, that represents a system or subsystem such as a host, back-end system, or line-of-business application to which you are connecting using SSO.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-160">分支應用程式代表非 Windows 系統，如大型主機或 UNIX 電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-160">An affiliate application can represent a non-Windows system such as a mainframe or UNIX computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-161">它也可以代表應用程式 (如 SAP)，或系統的子部分 (如 Benefits 或 Pay stub 子系統)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-161">It can also represent an application such as SAP, or a subdivision of the system, such as the "Benefits" or "Pay stub" sub-systems.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-162">agenda (議程)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-162">agenda</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-163">由規則引擎執行的排序規則動作清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-163">An ordered list of rule actions to be executed by the Rule Engine.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-164">彙總 (aggregation)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-164">aggregation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-165">資料表或結構，其中包含為線上分析處理 (OLAP) Cube 預先計算的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-165">A table or structure containing pre-calculated data for an online analytical processing (OLAP) cube.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-166">彙總支援以快速及有效率的方式查詢多維度資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-166">Aggregations support the rapid and efficient querying of a multidimensional database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-167">agreement (協議)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-167">agreement</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-168">關係組態中的闡述項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-168">The defining item in relationship configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-169">協議是以基礎的商務程序及合作對象管理成品為依據，而在您本身的設定檔與夥伴設定檔之間定義的，</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-169">An agreement is based on the underlying business process and party management artifacts, and is defined between your self profile and your partner’s profile.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-170">且由一或多個增補所組成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-170">It consists of one or more addendums.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-171">增補定義所使用的商務程序、貴組織和夥伴扮演的角色，以及關係中使用的參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-171">Addendums define the business process used, the role of your organization, your partner’s role, and the parameters used in the relationship.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-172">協議也可以參考夥伴群組設定檔而不參考個別的夥伴設定檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-172">Agreements can also refer to partner group profiles instead of individual partner profiles.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-173">這有助於管理和貴組織有完全相同的交易關係之所有夥伴。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-173">This facilitates the management of partners that have identical trading relationships with your organization.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-174">alert notification (警示通知)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-174">alert notification</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-175">用來通知使用者或一群使用者關於可顯示的特定預先定義情況的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-175">The means used to notify a user or a group of users about a specific predefined situation that could manifest.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-176">alias</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-176">alias</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-177">合作對象的別稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-177">A alternate way to refer to a party.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-178">每個合作對象各有其指定的預設別名，包含組織名稱、OrganizationName 的辨識符號，以及合作對象名稱的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-178">Each party is given a single default alias with a name of organization, a qualifier as OrganizationName, and value for the name of the party.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-179">此別名永遠視為預設別名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-179">This alias is always regarded as the default alias.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-180">別名是由名稱、辨識符號和值三項組合而成的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-180">Aliases are provided as triads of name, qualifier, and value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-181">同一個 BizTalk 管理資料庫中的兩個合作對象，不可擁有相同的辨識符號值組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-181">No two parties in the same BizTalk Management database can have the same qualifier value pair.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-182">All、FirstMatch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-182">All, FirstMatch</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-183">管線階段的兩種執行模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-183">Two types of execution modes for pipeline stages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-184">All 表示階段中管線元件的線性執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-184">All indicates the linear execution of pipeline components in the stage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-185">FirstMatch 表示探索執行，其中第一個識別出訊息格式的元件會使用該訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-185">FirstMatch indicates a probed execution in which the first component that recognizes the message format consumes the message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-186">在線性執行中，階段中所有元件都依序執行後，才會將訊息傳遞到下個階段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-186">In linear execution, all components in a stage are executed in order before the message is passed to the next stage.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-187">ANSI X.12</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-187">ANSI X.12</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-188">由美國國家標準局 (American National Standards Institute) 開發出來的訊息格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-188">A message format developed by the American National Standards Institute.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-189">美國主要使用 X.12 格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-189">X.12 is used primarily in the United States.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-190">應用程式配接器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-190">application adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-191">建立與特定應用程式或通訊協定 (如 SQL) 搭配使用的配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-191">An adapter created to work with a specific application or protocol, such as SQL.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-192">封存的資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-192">archived data</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-193">已經由 BizTalk Server 處理而且儲存於適當資料庫的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-193">Data that has been processed by BizTalk Server and stored in the appropriate database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-194">artifact (成品)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-194">artifact</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-195">最常稱為 BizTalk 應用程式的一部分 (此應用程式是 BizTalk 解決方案的一個邏輯單位)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-195">Most often referred to as a part of a BizTalk application, which is a logical unit for a BizTalk solution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-196">成品是透過 BizTalk Server 管理主控台進行管理和部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-196">Artifacts are managed and deployed through the BizTalk Administration console.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-197">範例包括協調流程、管線、訊息結構描述、安全性憑證、商務規則原則和繫結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-197">Examples are orchestrations, pipelines, message schemas, security certificates, business rule policies, and bindings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-198">成品也是 BizTalk 專案的一部分 (此專案是 BizTalk 解決方案的另一個邏輯單位)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-198">Artifacts are also the parts of a BizTalk project, another logical unit for a BizTalk solution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-199">在此內容中，成品是用來產生 Visual Studio 中組成 BizTalk 解決方案的組件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-199">In this context, the artifacts are used to generate the assemblies in Visual Studio that make up the BizTalk solution.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-200">assembler (組合器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-200">assembler</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-201">將個別文件結合到一個批次的管線元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-201">A pipeline component that combines individual documents into a batch.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-202">BizTalk Server 中提供的組合器管線元件包括一般檔案組合器、BizTalk Framework 組合器和 XML 組合器三種管線元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-202">Assembler pipeline components provided in BizTalk Server are Flat file assembler, BizTalk Framework Assembler, and XML Assembler pipeline components.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-203">組件 (assembly)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-203">assembly</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-204">BizTalk 應用程式中使用的 dll 檔案，內有協調流程、管線、結構描述、對應等資源，以及並非 BizTalk Server 特有的其他資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-204">A dll file that may contain resources, such as orchestrations, pipelines, schemas, maps, and other resources that are not BizTalk Server specific, to be used in a BizTalk application.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-205">assembly deployment (組件部署)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-205">assembly deployment</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-206">將組件的資源從 Visual Studio 部署至 BizTalk 應用程式的過程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-206">The process of deploying the resources of an assembly from Visual Studio into a BizTalk application.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-207">Assembly Deployment Wizard (組件部署精靈)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-207">Assembly Deployment Wizard</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-208">BizTalk Server 2004 提供的精靈，能引導您執行新增、移除、匯入和匯出組件；匯入和匯出繫結；以及安裝或解除安裝全域組件快取 (GAC) 內各組件的必要步驟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-208">In BizTalk Server 2004, a wizard that guided you through the steps required to add, remove, import and export assemblies; import and export bindings; and install or uninstall assemblies from the global assembly cache (GAC).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-209">在 [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)] 中，匯入精靈、安裝精靈和匯出精靈均不再提供此功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-209">In [!INCLUDE[btsBizTalkServerNoVersion](../includes/btsbiztalkservernoversion-md.md)], this functionality is not provided by the Import, Installation, and Export Wizards.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-210">assembly version (組件版本)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-210">assembly version</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-211">組件的識別項，由主要版本和次要版本組合而成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-211">An identifier for an assembly, made up of a combination of a major and a minor version.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-212">atomic orchestration (不可部分完成的協調流程)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-212">atomic orchestration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-213">短期生效的交易，強迫 ACID (Atomicity、Consistency、Isolation 和 Durability) 交易的認可和回復，與使用 DTC 服務的 COM+ 應用程式相似。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-213">A short-lived transaction that enforces the commit and rollback semantics of an ACID (Atomicity, Consistency, Isolation, and Durability) transaction similar to a COM+ application that uses the DTC service.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-214">屬性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-214">attribute</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-215">在 XML 中，用來關聯其他資訊與 XML 項目的 XML 建構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-215">In XML, an XML construct used to associate additional information with XML elements.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-216">信任的驗證</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-216">Authentication Trusted</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-217">標示每個應用程式的方法，指示應用程式可以提交訊息到訊息方塊，該訊息方塊的合作對象識別碼 (PID) 與應用程式執行個體服務帳戶的 Windows 安全性識別碼不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-217">A means of marking each application indicating that the application can submit messages into the message box with a Party ID (PID) that is different (that is, not aliased by) the Windows Security ID of the application instance service account.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="b"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-218">B</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-218">B</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-219">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-219">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-220">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-220">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-221">BAM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-221">BAM</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-222">請參閱 Business Activity Monitoring (BAM) (商務活動監控)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-222">See Business Activity Monitoring (BAM).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-223">BAM activity (BAM 活動)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-223">BAM activity</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-224">BAM 根據所要監控的工作單位而擷取的端對端里程碑和資料之清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-224">The end-to-end list of milestones and data captured by BAM for a unit of work to be monitored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-225">例如，貸款申請活動可能包含如「已核准貸款」的里程碑，以及如「申請者名稱」和「貸款金額」等資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-225">For example, a loan application activity might contain milestones such as “Loan approved” and data such as “Applicant name” and “Loan amount.”</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-226">BAM 活動通常直接對應到商務程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-226">BAM activities often map directly to a business process.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-227">BAM alert (BAM 警示)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-227">BAM alert</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-228">由 BAM 基礎結構 (特別是 SQL Server Notification Services) 所產生的通知，以提醒收件者有特定狀況發生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-228">A notification generated by the BAM infrastructure (specifically, by SQL Server Notification Services) to inform the recipient that a given set of conditions exists.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-229">使用者定義警示的條件，而自動化服務則在這些條件符合時產生警示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-229">Users define the conditions for an alert and then automated services generate the alert whenever those conditions are met.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-230">BAM checkpoint (BAM 檢查點)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-230">BAM checkpoint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-231">也稱為 Excel BAM 增益集中的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-231">Also known as an item in the BAM Add-in for Excel.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-232">BAM Configuration (BAM 組態)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-232">BAM Configuration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-233">含有 BAM 資訊清單之各項設定 (如 BAM 主要匯入資料庫和伺服器名稱) 的 XML 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-233">The XML file that contains the settings for BAM manifests such as the BAM Primary Import database and server names.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-234">BAM definition (BAM 定義)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-234">BAM definition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-235">BAM 觀察模型的 XML 表示法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-235">An XML representation of a BAM observation model.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-236">BAM Framework (BAM 架構)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-236">BAM Framework</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-237">一組受管理的 API，支援動態建立的基礎結構和事件集中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-237">A set of managed APIs that support dynamically created infrastructure and event concentration.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-238">BAM infrastructure (BAM 基礎結構)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-238">BAM infrastructure</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-239">由 BAM 資料庫 (主要匯入、封存、星狀結構描述和分析) 中的 SQL Server 資料表、BAM 檢視、預存程序以及 Data Transformation Services (DTS) 封裝所組成，這些項目是透過 BAM 定義的累加部署所設定和管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-239">Consists of SQL Server tables, BAM views, stored procedures, and Data Transformation Services (DTS) packages in the BAM databases (Primary Import, Archive, Star Schema, and Analysis) as configured and managed through incremental deployments of BAM definitions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-240">此基礎結構即是執行階段時，事件相互關聯、彙總，然後可供使用者查詢的地方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-240">The infrastructure is where, at run time, events are correlated, aggregated, and then made available for user queries.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-241">BAM Manager (BAM 管理員)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-241">BAM Manager</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-242">管理商務活動監控動態基礎結構的內部元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-242">The internal component that manages the dynamic infrastructure for Business Activity Monitoring.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-243">BAM observational model (BAM 觀察模型)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-243">BAM observational model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-244">商務程序中可見性需求的高階定義，詳細說明里程碑和蒐集的資料事件 (BAM 活動)、任何資料彙總的描述，以及向使用者呈現資訊的方式 (BAM 檢視)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-244">A high-level definition of visibility requirements for a business process that specifics the milestone and data events to collect (the BAM activity); a description of any data aggregations; and the presentation of information to users (the BAM view).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-245">BAM view (BAM 檢視)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-245">BAM view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-246">構成 BAM 活動的資料依特定角色區別的觀點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-246">A role-specific perspective on the data that constitutes a BAM activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-247">檢視中包含篩選的資料、所篩選資料的彙總，以及呈現篩選資料的方式，例如樞紐分析圖報表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-247">Views consist of filtered data, aggregations of the filtered data, and ways of presenting the filtered data, such as a PivotChart report.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-248">每個 BAM 活動支援一或多個檢視的定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-248">BAM supports the definition of one or more views per activity.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-249">base data item (基底資料項)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-249">base data item</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-250">在 BAM 中，做為維度或量值之基準的活動項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-250">In BAM, an Activity item that is used as a basis for a dimension or measure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-251">例如，基底資料項「產品識別碼」可做為「計數」量值 (特定產品銷售數量) 之基準。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-251">For example, the base data item  "product ID" could be used as the basis for a Count measure (how many of a given product was sold).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-252">繫結</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-252">binding</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-253">軟體元件與軟體層連結在一起的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-253">A process by which software components and layers are linked together.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-254">安裝網路元件時，便會建立元件的繫結關聯性與相依性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-254">When a network component is installed, the binding relationships and dependencies for the components are established.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-255">繫結使元件得以彼此通訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-255">Binding allows components to communicate with each other.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-256">在 BizTalk Server 中，此為協調流程配接器-不特定結束點 (連接埠或角色連結) 與實體配接器-特定結束點 (傳送埠/接收埠或合作對象) 之間的已建立對應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-256">In BizTalk Server, an established mapping between an orchestration adapter-agnostic endpoint (port or role link) and physical adapter-specific endpoints (send/receive ports or party).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-257">binding file (繫結檔案)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-257">binding file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-258">包含繫結之快照的檔案，此快照正是擷取當時的繫結狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-258">A file that contains a snapshot of the binding as seen at that instant.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-259">它不包含與協調流程相關的繫結的完整細節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-259">It does not contain details about the completeness of the binding with respect to the orchestration.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-260">BizTalk Administration console (BizTalk 管理主控台)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-260">BizTalk Administration console</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-261">用來管理 BizTalk Server 群組的 Microsoft Management Console (MMC)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-261">A Microsoft Management Console (MMC) used to administer a BizTalk Server group.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-262">BizTalk Administrators group (BizTalk 系統管理員群組)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-262">BizTalk Administrators group</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-263">管理 BizTalk Server 的群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-263">The group that administers BizTalk Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-264">管理工作包括存取訊息擱置佇列、更新組態資料庫等等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-264">Administrative tasks include accessing the Suspended queue, updating the Configuration database, and so on.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-265">BizTalk application (BizTalk 應用程式)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-265">BizTalk application</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-266">集中公開的一組相關成品、資源及設定，可從 BizTalk 管理主控台內部進行管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-266">A group of related artifacts, resources, and settings that are exposed together for management from within the BizTalk Administration console.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-267">應用程式中的任何成品可能參考該應用程式中的其他任一成品，甚至參考任何所參考之應用程式中的任一成品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-267">Any artifact within an application may refer to any other artifact within that application, as well as any artifact in any referenced application.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-268">BizTalk Application 1 (BizTalk 應用程式 1)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-268">BizTalk Application 1</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-269">每次全新安裝 BizTalk Server 時預設建立的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-269">The application created by default in every new BizTalk Server installation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-270">建立此應用程式主要是基於回溯相容性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-270">This application is created mainly for backwards compatibility.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-271">部署時未指定應用程式的成品均顯示於此資料夾中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-271">Artifacts that were deployed without an application specified are shown in this folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-272">此外，未指定應用程式的新成品一律部署至 [預設應用程式]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-272">Also, new artifacts that are deployed without an application specified are deployed to the Default Application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-273">其他任何應用程式則可藉由變更使用者設定而設定為預設應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-273">Any other application may be set as the default by changing a user setting.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-274">BizTalk Application Users group (BizTalk 應用程式使用者群組)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-274">BizTalk Application Users group</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-275">可以存取特定 BizTalk 群組的 MessageBox 的使用者群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-275">The group of users who can access MessageBoxes for a particular BizTalk Group</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-276">BizTalk Application view (BizTalk 應用程式檢視)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-276">BizTalk Application view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-277">開啟 BizTalk Server 的 System Center Operations Manager 主控台時所顯示的兩個檢視之一 (另一個是 [BizTalk 部署檢視])。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-277">One of two views (along with BizTalk Deployment View) that appears when the System Center Operations Manager console for BizTalk Server is opened.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-278">BizTalk 系統管理員會使用這個檢視來監視 BizTalk Server 成品和應用程式的健全狀況，如協調流程、傳送埠和接收位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-278">A BizTalk administrator uses this view to monitor the health of BizTalk artifacts and applications such as orchestrations, send ports, and receive locations.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-291">BizTalk Explorer Object Model (BizTalk 總管物件模型)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-291">BizTalk Explorer Object Model</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-292">用來建立工具和指令碼的 API，可以自動化在 BizTalk 總管中執行的後部署工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-292">The APIs used to create tools and scripts to automate the post-deployment tasks that you perform in BizTalk Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-293">您可以將 BizTalk 總管物件模型用於後續部署工作，例如建立連接埠、繫結協調流程、管理合作對象屬性，或是任何其他會用到 BizTalk 總管的工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-293">You can use the BizTalk Explorer Object Model for such post-deployment tasks as creating ports, binding orchestrations, managing party properties, or any other task where you would use BizTalk Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-294">BizTalk 總管物件模型 API 位於 Microsoft.BizTalk.ExplorerOM 命名空間內。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-294">The BizTalk Explorer Object Model APIs are in the Microsoft.BizTalk.ExplorerOM namespace.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-295">BizTalk Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-295">BizTalk Framework</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-296">一種平台中性電子商務架構，以延伸標記語言 (XML) 結構描述和產業標準為建構基礎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-296">A platform-neutral e-commerce framework that is based on Extensible Markup Language (XML) schemas and industry standards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-297">這種架構可以整合產業和各種商務系統，無論平台、作業系統或基礎技術為何。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-297">The framework enables integration across industries and between business systems, regardless of platform, operating system, or underlying technology.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-298">BizTalk 群組</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-298">BizTalk group</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-299">包含 MessageBox、主控件、接收位置、傳送埠、傳送埠群組、協調流程、伺服器和配接器的群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-299">A group that contains MessageBoxes, hosts, receive locations, send ports, send port groups, orchestrations, servers, and adapters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-300">BizTalk host (BizTalk 主控件)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-300">BizTalk host</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-301">BizTalk Server 中的邏輯程序與安全性界限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-301">A logical process and security boundary within BizTalk Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-302">每個主控件各有其指派的安全性群組，並且可能包含多個主控件執行個體，分別位於不同的電腦以執行該主控件的工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-302">Each host has a security group assigned to it and may contain multiple host instances, each on an individual machine, that perform the work of the host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-303">因而，每個主控件執行個體均隸屬於單一主控件，主控件執行個體的服務帳戶則隸屬於該主控件的安全性群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-303">In turn, each host instance belongs to exactly one host, and the service account of the host instance belongs to the security group of the host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-304">安全性群組可用來授與主控件的任一主控件執行個體使用實體資源 (如資料庫) 的權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-304">The security group may be used to grant permissions to physical resources such as databases for use by any host instances in the host.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-305">BizTalk Management Pack alert (BizTalk 管理封包警示)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-305">BizTalk Management Pack alert</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-306">系統管理員可以在 BizTalk Server 管理組件中訂閱通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-306">A notification that administrators can subscribe to in the BizTalk Server Management Pack.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-307">訂閱某個警示之後，只要符合特定條件，系統管理員就會收到通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-307">After subscribing to a given alert, administrators receive a notification whenever certain conditions are met.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-308">例如，若進行節流的主控件執行個體達到特定數目，即可能引發警示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-308">For instance, if a certain number of host instances are throttling, an alert could be raised.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-309">BizTalk Management Pack diagnostics (BizTalk 管理封包診斷)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-309">BizTalk Management Pack diagnostics</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-310">系統管理員可以使用這項功能來查看某個問題的原因和疑難排解資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-310">A feature that administrators can use to see the cause and troubleshooting information for a given problem.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-311">例如，若傳送埠的健全狀況呈現紅色，則 Operations Manager 主控台的 [狀態變更事件] 索引標籤會顯示健全狀況由綠變紅的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-311">For example, if the health of a send port appears as red, the State Change Event tab in the Operations Manager console displays the reason why it went from green to red.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-406">Composition service (組合服務)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-406">Composition service</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-407">處理動作啟動、干擾功能和工作回應傳送的元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-407">The component that handles the action activation, interrupt functionality, and the sending of task responses.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-408">服務會組成動作通訊協定訊息，再將它們傳送到 HTTP 待命程式，接著傳送到 MessageBox 資料庫以供取用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-408">The service composes the action protocol messages and sends them to the HTTP listeners which then rout them into the MessageBox database for consumption.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-409">condition (條件)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-409">condition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-410">規則的 "IF" 部分，用來指定應該要評估的條件，也就是以評估為真或假的單一邏輯運算式來表示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-410">The "IF" part of a rule, used to specify what conditions should be evaluated, that is, represented using a single logical expression that evaluates to true or false.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-411">條件可以延伸以支援使用者定義條件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-411">A condition is extensible to support user-defined conditions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-412">configuration cache refresh Interval (組態快取重新整理間隔)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-412">configuration cache refresh Interval</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-413">收取 BizTalk 群組 (如 SMTP 主機) 的一般屬性所做之變更的秒數間隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-413">The interval, in seconds,  in which changes to general properties for a BizTalk group, such as the SMTP host, are picked up.).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-414">此間隔設定為群組組態的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-414">This interval is set as part of group configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-415">當 BizTalk Server 啟動後，BizTalk Server 管理中所有的項目 (例如：MessageBox 資料庫、伺服器屬性、配接器以及追蹤資料庫的連線) 均儲存於管理快取中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-415">When you start BizTalk Server, all items in BizTalk Server Administration, such as MessageBox databases, server properties, adapters, and connections to the Tracking database, are stored in the administration cache.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-416">根據預設，快取中所有的項目每隔 60 秒會重新整理一次，但伺服器資料庫連線和伺服器屬性除外。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-416">By default, all items in the cache are refreshed every 60 seconds, except for the server database connections and server properties.</span></span>|
