|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-426">以內容為基礎的路由</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-426">content-based routing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-427">根據從文件內容擷取的資訊作為文件路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-427">The routing of a document based on the information extracted from the payload of the document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-428">在 BizTalk Server 中，在傳送埠和協調流程上使用文件屬性升級和篩選條件運算式，可以進行以內容為基礎的路由。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-428">In BizTalk Server, content-based routing is achieved by using document property promotion and filter expressions on send ports and orchestrations.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-429">continuation (接續)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-429">continuation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-430">指使用兩個不同的唯一識別碼作為 ActivityID，從不同的應用程式完成單一 BAM 活動的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-430">The ability to contribute to a single BAM activity from different applications by using two different unique identifiers as the ActivityID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-431">例如，在商務程序的某一部分中，可能會使用客戶的訂單號碼來追蹤某項活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-431">For example, in one part of a business process, a customer’s PO number might be used to track an activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-432">在該程序的另一個部分中，則可能會使用內部訂單履行號碼來追蹤同一項活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-432">In another part of the process, an internal order fulfillment number might be used to track the same activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-433">您可以啟用接續功能，並使訂單號碼與訂單履行號碼產生關聯，如此一來，該程序的兩個部分便可以新增資訊到同一項活動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-433">You could enable continuation and relate the PO number and the order fulfillment number, so that both parts of the process could add information to the same activity.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-434">Continuation token (接續 Token)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-434">Continuation token</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-435">從「應用程式 1」送出的一段唯一資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-435">A piece of unique information that is sent out of Application 1.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-436">conversion rate (轉換率)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-436">conversion rate</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-437">用於將網站的基準貨幣轉換成買方貨幣或供應商貨幣的乘數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-437">The multiplier used for converting the base currency of the Web site to the buyer currency or supplier currency.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-438">儲存於 SDK Order Sitelet 中的轉換率僅供示範用途，且應交由具有公信力的第三方或生產網站上的會計系統定期追蹤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-438">The conversion rate is stored in the SDK Order Sitelet for illustrative purposes only, and should be tracked by a third party fulfillment or accounting system in production Web sites.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-439">correlation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-439">correlation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-440">指將內送訊息對應到適當協調流程執行個體的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-440">The process of matching an incoming message with the appropriate instance of an orchestration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-441">此對應是透過訊息中使訊息連結到協調流程的屬性來進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-441">This matching occurs through properties of the message that link it to the orchestration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-442">如果與同一個商務程序有關的訊息包含不相容的屬性 (例如訂單結構描述具有 POId 項目，而搭配的發票結構描述具有 OrderID 項目)，則開發人員會透過建立屬性結構描述，並讓這些屬性結構描述包含這些項目的抽象化屬性名稱，來達到相互關聯的目的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-442">In cases where messages related to the same business process contain incompatible properties, such as a purchase order schema with an element POId, and a companion invoice schema with an element OrderID, developers achieve the correlation by creating property schemas that contain abstracted property names for these elements.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-443">correlation ID (相互關聯識別碼)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-443">correlation ID</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-444">隨機產生的識別碼，與訊息關聯，並隨著指定訊息的存續期一起傳遞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-444">A randomly generated ID that is associated with a message and passed along for the lifetime of a given message.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-445">correlation set (相互關聯集合)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-445">correlation set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-446">相互關聯類型的執行個體；也就是用來決定訊息是否屬於協調流程指定執行個體的列出屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-446">An instance of a correlation type; that is, the listed properties for a message that are used to determine whether it belongs to a given instance of an orchestration.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-447">correlation type (相互關聯類型)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-447">correlation type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-448">一組訊息屬性，做為商業程序的唯一識別，用來相互關聯訊息與協調流程執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-448">A set of message properties that uniquely identify a business process and that are used to correlate messages with orchestration instances.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-449">culture (文化特性)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-449">culture</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-450">文字和資料的語言及可當地語系化的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-450">The language and localizable properties of text and data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-451">custom adapter (自訂配接器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-451">custom adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-452">由開發人員撰寫的自訂程式碼，放在接收管線之前或傳送管線之後，當作配接器和 (或) 應用程式的介面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-452">A custom piece of code that a developer writes and places before a receive pipeline or after a send pipeline to interface with adapters and/or applications.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-453">custom numbers (自訂編號)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-453">custom numbers</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-454">由計數器指派的編號數列，每個編號的值以一為單位遞增。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-454">A series of numbers assigned by a counter that increases the value of each number by one.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-455">cyclical reference (循環參考)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-455">cyclical reference</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-456">XML 結構描述的模式，其中子系節點宣告為與其中上階節點的相同複雜類型，因此可以建立可以有無限深度、表示執行個體訊息的結構描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-456">A pattern in an XML schema in which a descendant node is declared to be of the same complex type as one of its ancestor nodes, thereby creating a schema that represents instance messages with potentially unlimited depth.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="d"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-457">D</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-457">D</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-458">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-458">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-459">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-459">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-460">Data Description Language (DDL) (資料描述語言)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-460">Data Description Language (DDL)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-461">用來定義資料及其與其他資料之關係的語言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-461">A language used to define data and its relationships to other data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-462">用來在資料庫內建立資料結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-462">It is used to create the data structure in a database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-463">多數資料庫管理系統 (DBMS) 都使用 SQL 資料描述語言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-463">Major database management systems (DBMSs) use a SQL data description language.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-464">data dimension (資料維度)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-464">data dimension</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-465">在追蹤設定檔編輯器建立為階層式檢視的特定節點，做為特定追蹤設定檔的直接子系，以便描述邏輯群組或資料維度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-465">A specific node created in the hierarchical view of the Tracking Profile Editor as an immediate child of the specific tracking profile in order to describe a logical grouping or dimension of data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-466">每個資料維度都有唯一名字，而且由一或多個資料欄位組成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-466">Each data dimension is uniquely named and is made up of one or many data fields.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-467">data item (資料項目)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-467">data item</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-468">在追蹤設定檔編輯器中建立為階層式檢視的特定節點，為資料類別的直接子系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-468">A specific node created in the hierarchical view of the Tracking Profile Editor that is a direct child of Data Category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-469">資料欄位存在為商務內容的特定欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-469">The data field exists as a specific field from the business payload.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-470">data mapping (資料對應)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-470">data mapping</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-471">設計階段程序，定義來源結構描述中節點與目的結構描述中節點之間的對應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-471">The design-time process of defining a mapping between nodes in a source schema and nodes in a destination schema.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-472">DDL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-472">DDL</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-473">請參閱 Data Description Language (資料描述語言)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-473">See Data Description Language.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-474">default host (預設主控件)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-474">default host</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-475">方便部署和協調流程登錄的管理物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-475">Administration objects that facilitate deployment and orchestration enlistment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-476">這些物件在 BizTalk Server 管理主控台中以核選符號加以識別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-476">These objects are identified in the BizTalk Server Administration console with a checkmark symbol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-477">在協調流程登錄程序期間，會自動使用預設主控件來裝載協調流程，除非使用者明確選取不同的主控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-477">During the orchestration enlistment process, the default host is automatically used to host the orchestration, unless the user explicitly selects a different host.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-478">default pipelines (預設管線)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-478">default pipelines</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-479">已編譯且部署的 BizTalk Server 組件，包含已設定階段的管線及管線元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-479">The compiled and deployed BizTalk Server assemblies that contain pipelines with preconfigured stages and pipeline components.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-480">dehydrate (凍結)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-480">dehydrate</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-481">當協調流程閒置特定時間後，用來將正在執行的協調流程狀態儲存至永久存放區，並從記憶體中移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-481">Saving the state of a running orchestration to persistent storage and removing it from memory when the orchestration has been idle for a certain length of time.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-482">delimited flat file (分隔式一般檔案)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-482">delimited flat file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-483">用來表示商務文件的檔案格式類型，其中記錄和記錄內的欄位會以特定字元或字元序列加以分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-483">A type of file format used to represent business documents in which the records and fields within the records are delimited by specific characters or sequence of characters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-484">分隔符號 (delimiter)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-484">delimiter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-485">一或多個特殊字元，在任何層級 (欄位、記錄等) 的分隔結構中用來分隔同層物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-485">One or more special characters that are used to separate peers in a delimited structure, at any level (fields, records, and so on).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-486">demotion (降級)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-486">demotion</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-487">從內容屬性將日期/時間資料撰寫到文件內容裡的動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-487">The act of writing date/time data from a context property into the document payload.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-488">Destination database (目的資料庫)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-488">Destination database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-489">與 BizTalk Server 一起安裝時唯一支援的目的資料庫，儘管 BAM 事件匯流排服務基礎結構支援多個目的資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-489">When installed with BizTalk Server, the only destination that is supported, although multiple Destination databases are supported by the BAM Event Bus Service infrastructure.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-490">destination schema (目的結構描述)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-490">destination schema</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-491">BizTalk Server 對應中使用的結構描述，表示輸出執行個體訊息的結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-491">The schema used in a BizTalk Server map that represents the structure of the output message instances.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-492">Development Tools Environment (DTE) (開發工具環境)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-492">Development Tools Environment (DTE)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-493">讓開發人員能以程式設計方式透過整合式開發環境 (IDE) 達成許多主要工作的一組介面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-493">A set of interfaces that enable developers to programmatically achieve several of the key tasks achievable from the Integrated Development Environment (IDE).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-494">維度階層</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-494">dimension hierarchy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-495">一種邏輯樹狀結構，它將維度的各個成員組織起來，使每個成員都有一個父成員及零或多個子成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-495">A logical tree structure that organizes the members of a dimension such that each member has one parent member and zero or more child members.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-496">維度層級</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-496">dimension level</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-497">指出一組資料項目視為是維度階層各層級的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-497">An element that indicates that a set of data items are to be considered as levels of a dimension hierarchy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-498">DataPerspective 定義是由 OLAP 維度階層所產生的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-498">The DataPerspective definition results in an OLAP Dimension Hierarchy.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-499">disassembler pipeline component (解譯器管線元件)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-499">disassembler pipeline component</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-500">將一批訊息分開到個別文件的管線元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-500">A pipeline component that divides messages in a batch into individual documents.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-501">BizTalk Server 所提供的解譯器管線元件包括：一般檔案解譯器、BizTalk Framework 解譯器和 XML 解譯器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-501">The disassembler pipeline components provided in BizTalk Server are: Flat file disassembler, BizTalk Framework disassembler, and XML disassembler.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-502">distinguished field (辨別欄位)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-502">distinguished field</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-503">訊息中的 .NET 類別成員或 XML 結構描述定義語言 (XSD) 結構描述欄位，已明確提供給協調流程用於運算式及自訂管線元件中，做為寫入的屬性欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-503">A .NET class member or XML Schema Definition language (XSD) schema field in a message that has been explicitly made available to an orchestration for use in expressions and custom pipeline components as a written property field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-504">不能用於篩選條件運算式中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-504">It cannot be used in filter expressions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-505">distributed transaction coordinator (DTC) (分散式交易協調器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-505">distributed transaction coordinator (DTC)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-506">與 COM+ 整合的服務，讓分散式交易可以運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-506">A service, integrated with COM+, that makes distributed transactions work.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="cc989-507">DTC 讓交易可以從一個電腦延展到許多電腦上，而不需要特別的程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-507">DTC makes it possible to scale transactions from one to many computers without the need for special code.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-508">DMZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-508">DMZ</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-509">周邊網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-509">Demilitarized zone.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-510">請參閱 perimeter network (周邊網路)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-510">See perimeter network.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-511">document (文件)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-511">document</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-512">在 EDI 中為一組邏輯結合的區段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-512">In EDI, a set of logically combined segments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-513">文件類型包括：發票、運輸訂單、客戶宣告等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-513">Types of documents include: invoices, transportation orders, customs declarations, and so on.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-514">文件類型定義 (DTD)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-514">document type definition (DTD)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-515">可以描述 XML 文件結構的數種方式之一。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-515">One of several ways in which the structure of an XML document can be described.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-516">BizTalk Server 可以開啟以 DTD 描述的結構描述，並在程序中將它轉換為 XSD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-516">BizTalk Server can open a schema described using a DTD, but converts it to XSD in the process.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-517">DTC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-517">DTC</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-518">請參閱 distributed transaction coordinator (DTC) (分散式交易協調器)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-518">See distributed transaction coordinator (DTC).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-519">DTD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-519">DTD</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-520">請參閱 document type definition (DTD) (文件類型定義)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-520">See document type definition (DTD).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-521">DTE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-521">DTE</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-522">請參閱 Development Tools Environment (DTE) (開發工具環境)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-522">See Development Tools Environment (DTE).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-523">duration</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-523">duration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-524">指示 BAM 編譯器在表示檢查點之間持續時間的檢視中建立其他資料行的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-524">An element that instructs the BAM Compiler to create additional column in the View that represents the duration between checkpoints.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-525">dynamic adapter (動態配接器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-525">dynamic adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-526">有自訂使用者介面的配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-526">An adapter that has a custom user interface.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-527">dynamic binding (動態繫結)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-527">dynamic binding</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-528">在執行階段套用到連接埠的連接埠繫結，一般是從訊息屬性 (如回覆位址) 衍生來的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-528">A port binding that is applied to the port at run time, typically derived from a message property such as a reply-to address.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-529">dynamic policy update (動態原則更新)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-529">dynamic policy update</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-530">使用規則引擎更新服務在執行階段擷取原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-530">The run-time retrieval of policies using the Rule Engine Update service.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-531">dynamic port (動態連接埠)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-531">dynamic port</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-532">沒有目的位址也沒有關聯的配接器類型的傳送埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-532">A send port that does not have a destination address and adapter type associated with it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-533">動態傳送埠允許在執行階段執行期間將其自身與目的位址和配接器類型建立關聯，因此提供使用相同連接埠傳送訊息至使用不同配接器類型的目的彈性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-533">A dynamic send port allows the association of the destination address and adapter type with itself during runtime execution, thus providing flexibility in using the same port for sending messages to different destinations using different adapter types.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="e"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-534">E</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-534">E</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-535">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-535">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-536">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-536">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-537">EDI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-537">EDI</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-538">請參閱 electronic data interchange (EDI) (電子資料交換)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-538">See electronic data interchange (EDI).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-539">EDIFACT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-539">EDIFACT</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-540">請參閱 Electronic Data Interchange for Administration, Commerce and Trade (EDIFACT) (管理、商務和商業的電子資料交換)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-540">See Electronic Data Interchange for Administration, Commerce and Trade (EDIFACT).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-541">EDIFACT UNOA syntax (EDIFACT UNOA 語法)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-541">EDIFACT UNOA syntax</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-542">僅允許下列的 EDIFACT 語法字元： 大寫字母、 所有數字，保留空白，驚嘆號 （！）、 引號 （"）、 百分比符號 （%）、 連字號 (&)、 左和右括號 ("("and")")、 星號 （\*）、 逗號、 虛線 （-），小數點 （.），斜線 （/）、 分號 （;），較不-符號 (\<)，和更新版本-符號 (\>)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-542">An EDIFACT syntax that allows the following characters only: uppercase letters, all digits, blank, exclamation mark (!), quotation mark ("), percentage sign (%), ampersand (&), opening and closing parentheses ( "(" and ")"), asterisk (\*), comma, dash (-), decimal point (.), forward slash (/), semicolon (;), less-than sign (\<), and greater-than sign (\>).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-543">EDIFACT UNOB syntax (EDIFACT UNOB 語法)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-543">EDIFACT UNOB syntax</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-544">僅字元可讓下列的 EDIFACT 語法： 小寫及大寫字母、 所有數字，保留空白，驚嘆號 （！）、 引號 （"）、 百分比符號 （%）、 連字號 (&)、 單一引號 （'）、 左右括號 （"（"和")")、 星號 （\*）、 加號 （+）、 逗號、 虛線 （-）、 小數點 （.）、 可轉送斜線 （/）、 冒號 （:）、 分號 （;），較不-符號 (\<)，等號 （=）、 大於-符號 (\>)，和問號 （？）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-544">An EDIFACT syntax that allows the following characters only: lowercase and uppercase letters, all digits, blank, exclamation mark (!), quotation mark ("), percentage sign (%), ampersand (&), single quotation mark ('), opening and closing parentheses ( "(" and ")"), asterisk (\*), plus sign (+), comma, dash (-), decimal point (.), forward slash (/), colon (:), semicolon (;), less-than sign (\<), equal sign (=), greater-than sign (\>), and question mark (?).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-545">EIF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-545">EIF</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-546">請參閱 Engine Input File (EIF) (引擎輸入檔)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-546">See Engine Input File (EIF).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-547">EIP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-547">EIP</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-548">請參閱 Enterprise Integration Platform (EIP) (企業應用系統整合平台)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-548">See Enterprise Integration Platform (EIP).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-549">electronic data interchange (EDI) (電子資料交換)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-549">electronic data interchange (EDI)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-550">兩台電腦應用程式之間已建立結構及標準化文件的電子交換，使用一組標準來控制電腦之間文件的傳輸，例如訂單及發票。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-550">The electronic exchange of structured and normalized documents between two computer applications, using a set of standards to control the transfer of documents, such as purchase orders and invoices, between computers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-551">Electronic Data Interchange for Administration, Commerce and Trade (EDIFACT) (管理、商務和商業的電子資料交換)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-551">Electronic Data Interchange for Administration, Commerce and Trade (EDIFACT)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-552">全世界的電子資料交換 (EDI)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-552">A worldwide electronic data interchange (EDI)</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-553">element</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-553">element</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-554">在 EDI 中文件中的最低層級資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-554">In EDI, the lowest level of information in a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-555">例如，發票編號。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-555">For example, invoice number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-556">在 XML 中，以階層方式組織資訊的 XML 建構，在其他項目內套疊一些項目，具有無限深度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-556">In XML, an XML construct used to organize information in a hierarchical manner by nesting some elements within other elements to a potentially unlimited depth.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-557">element groups (項目群組)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-557">element groups</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-558">XML 結構中同層級項目的群組，依不同的條件約束分組：順序序列 (序列群組)、無順序序列 (所有群組) 以及一對多 (選擇群組)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-558">Groupings of sibling elements in an XML structure according to different constraints: ordered sequence (Sequence Group), unordered sequence (All Group), and one-of-many (Choice Group).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-559">encoding agreement (編碼協議)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-559">encoding agreement</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-560">指兩個交易夥伴的商務設定檔之間，規定要使用特定編碼通訊協定 (X12 或 EDIFACT) 來交換訊息的協議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-560">An agreement between the business profiles of two trading partners to use a specific encoding protocol (X12 or EDIFACT) while exchanging messages.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-561">encoding protocol (編碼通訊協定)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-561">encoding protocol</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-562">指負責控管 B2B 訊息結構和內容的通訊協定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-562">A protocol that governs the structure and content of a business-to-business message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-563">商務設定檔的編碼通訊協定設定會定義商務部門用來傳送和接收 B2B 訊息的編碼通訊協定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-563">The encoding protocol settings for a business profile define the encoding protocol that a business division uses to send and receive business-to-business messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-564">編碼通訊協定的一些範例包括 X12、EDIFACT、HIPAA 和 EANCOM。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-564">Some examples of encoding protocols are X12, EDIFACT, HIPAA, and EANCOM.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-565">加密金鑰</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-565">encryption key</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-566">用來加密或解密認證資訊的字串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-566">A string used to encrypt or decrypt credentials information.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-567">end type change request (結束類型變更要求)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-567">end type change request</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-568">使用管理主控台或 BTSTask 匯入 BizTalk 應用程式 MSI 檔案期間，將成品類型部署至目的端電腦的最後階段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-568">The last stage of the deployment of an artifact type onto the destination computer, during an import of a BizTalk application MSI file using the Administration console or BTSTask.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-569">也稱為認可變更要求，或認可匯入特定成品類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-569">Also known as a commit change request, or commit import for a type of artifact.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-570">端點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-570">endpoint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-571">位置的邏輯表示法，一般以 URL 形式表達，為擷取或傳送的資料提供實體位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-571">The logical representation of a location, typically expressed in URL form, providing a physical address for data received or sent.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-572">Engine Input File (EIF) (引擎輸入檔)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-572">Engine Input File (EIF)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-573">文件結構描述的編譯版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-573">A compiled version of a document schema.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-574">EIF 用來促進翻譯，在非公開使用者群組內其他使用者之間散佈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-574">The EIF is used to expedite translations for distribution among other users in a closed user group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-575">只要使用 BizTalk Server 產生或編輯 XML 結構描述定義語言 (XSD) 結構描述，就會自動編譯 EIF。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-575">The EIF is automatically compiled whenever an XML Schema Definition language (XSD) schema is generated or edited, using BizTalk Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-576">enlist (登錄)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-576">enlist</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-577">將協調流程與其執行所在實體環境建立關聯的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-577">The process of associating an orchestration with the physical environment in which it will run.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-578">其中包括：指定傳輸訊息到協調流程或從協調流程傳輸訊息所需的配接器、指定用於裝載協調流程的應用程式程序，並建立路由指示的 MessageBox 訂閱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-578">This includes specifying  the adapters needed to transport messages to and from the orchestration, the application process in which the orchestration is hosted, and creating the MessageBox subscriptions indicated by the routing.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-579">enterprise application integration (企業應用程式整合)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-579">enterprise application integration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-580">將企業應用程式中的資料或功能與其他應用程式中的資料或功能結合在一起的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-580">The process of bringing data or a function from an enterprise application together with that of another application.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-581">Enterprise Integration Platform (EIP) (企業應用系統整合平台)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-581">Enterprise Integration Platform (EIP)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-582">企業應用程式進行整合的環境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-582">The environment in which enterprise application integration occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-583">此實例實際是將同類的實例群組成單一實例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-583">This scenario is actually a class of scenarios grouped together as a single scenario.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-584">Enterprise Single Sign-On system (企業單一登入系統)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-584">Enterprise Single Sign-On system</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-585">SSO 資料庫、主要密碼伺服器以及一或多個企業單一登入 (SSO) 伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-585">An SSO database, a master secret server, and one or more Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO) servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-586">這些伺服器會在 Windows 與非 Windows 認證間進行對應，在 SSO 資料庫中尋找認證，然後用來管理 SSO 系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-586">These servers do the mapping between the Windows and non-Windows credentials, look up the credentials in the SSO database, and are used for administering the SSO system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-587">SSO 資料庫也做為組態存放區，保留配接器的自訂組態資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-587">The SSO database is also used as a configuration store to hold custom configuration data for adapters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-588">envelope (信封)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-588">envelope</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-589">有結構的一組資訊，包裝並伴隨執行個體訊息，通常是用來描述傳遞和處理資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-589">A structured set of information that wraps and accompanies an instance message, often describing delivery and processing information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-590">信封可以巢狀堆疊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-590">Envelopes can be nested.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-591">envelope schema (信封結構描述)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-591">envelope schema</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-592">結構描述的類型，指定信封的結構，使用信封專用的數個額外屬性，指定諸如識別信封資料流中信封內容的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-592">A type of schema that specifies the structure of an envelope, using several extra properties that are specific to envelopes and which specify information such as identifying the envelope contents in an enveloped data stream.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-593">execution cycle (執行循環)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-593">execution cycle</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-594">商務規則引擎內的事實判斷提示、條件評估和動作執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-594">The assertion of facts, evaluation of conditions, and execution of actions within the Business Rule Engine.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-595">執行模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-595">Execution Mode</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-596">管線階段屬性，決定階段中管線元件的執行模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-596">A pipeline stage property that determines the execution pattern of pipeline components in a stage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-597">執行模式可以設定為「全部」或「第一個符合的階段」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-597">The Execution Mode can be set to All or First Match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-598">在「全部」模式下，階段內的所有元件會依設定的序列依次執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-598">In All mode, all the components within the stage are carried out in the configured sequence.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-599">當需要數個元件完成特定邏輯工作，且必須全部執行時，請使用此模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-599">This mode is used when several components are required to complete a certain logical task, and they must all be executed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-600">如果任何元件在處理此管線階段的訊息時碰到錯誤，就會發生執行階段錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-600">If any component encounters an error while processing a message that is going through this pipeline stage, a run-time error results.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-601">Export Wizard (匯出精靈)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-601">Export Wizard</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-602">從 BizTalk 管理主控台啟動的精靈，用於從 BizTalk 應用程式產生 MSI 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-602">A wizard that you start from the BizTalk Administration Console to generate an MSI file from a BizTalk application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-603">接著便可將此 MSI 檔案複製到不同的 BizTalk Server 執行個體，然後使用匯入精靈來匯入 MSI 檔案的資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-603">You can then copy this MSI file to a different instance of BizTalk Server and use the Import Wizard to import the resources of the MSI file.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-604">express delivery (快遞)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-604">express delivery</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-605">暗指永久性 (儲存於 SQL 資料庫內) 的訊息傳遞類型，指內送訊息及外寄訊息兩者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-605">A type of message delivery that implies persistency (store in the SQL database), both for incoming messages and outgoing messages.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-606">可延伸樣式表語言轉換 (XSLT)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-606">Extensible Stylesheet Language Transformations (XSLT)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-607">從原先的 Extensible Stylesheet Language (XSL) 標準進化而來。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-607">Evolved from the early Extensible Stylesheet Language (XSL) standard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-608">XSL 指定 XML 資料簡報和資料轉換的語言定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-608">XSL specifies a language definition for XML data presentation and data transformations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-609">資料簡報表示以某種格式和 (或) 媒體顯示資料，並與樣式有關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-609">Data presentation means displaying data in some format and/or medium, and concerns style.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-610">資料轉換則是指將輸入 XML 文件剖析到節點樹狀結構，接著再將來源樹狀結構轉換為結果樹狀結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-610">Data transformation refers to parsing an input XML document into a tree of nodes, and then converting the source tree into a result tree.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-611">轉換與資料交換有關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-611">Transformation concerns data exchange.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-612">external message format (外部訊息格式)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-612">external message format</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-613">由 BizTalk Server 處理之前或之後的訊息格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-613">The format of the message before or after it is processed by BizTalk Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-614">指稱外部訊息格式時有時候也會使用 "wire" 格式一詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-614">Sometimes the term "wire" format is also used when referring to external message format.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="f"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-615">F</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-615">F</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-616">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-616">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-617">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-617">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-618">facet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-618">facet</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-619">XML 結構描述定義語言 (XSD) 概念，限制項目或屬性可以採用的值，為結構描述的執行個體提供驗證參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-619">An XML Schema Definition language (XSD) concept for restricting the possible values that an element or attribute can take, providing validation parameters for instances of a schema.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-620">例如，可以指定字串資料的最小及最大長度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-620">For example, a minimum and maximum length can be specified for string data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-621">不同類型的 facet 套用至不同類型的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-621">Different types of facets apply to different types of data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-622">事實</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-622">fact</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-623">套用規則條件的使用者資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-623">User data to which rule conditions are applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-624">在設計階段，事實是該資料的參考。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-624">At design time a fact is a reference to that data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-625">fact base (事實資料庫)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-625">fact base</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-626">評估規則條件所根據的事實集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-626">A collection of facts against which rule conditions are evaluated.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-627">fact retriever (事實擷取器 (規則引擎))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-627">fact retriever (Rule Engine)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-628">實作 IFactRetriever 介面、由使用者定義的選擇性外掛程式元件，因此可收集長期事實以供商務原則使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-628">An optional, user-defined plug-in component that implements an IFactRetriever interface so that it can gather long-term facts for use by business policies.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-629">fact store (事實存放區)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-629">fact store</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-630">儲存執行者的資訊 (包括角色和屬性) 的資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-630">The database that stores information, including role and attributes, about actors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-631">事實存放區也提供階層式巡覽，這樣動作可以決定組織內執行者的相對位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-631">The fact store also provides hierarchy navigation so that actions can determine the relative positions of actors within an organization.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-632">fact store manager (事實存放區管理員)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-632">fact store manager</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-633">從各種 FactRetriever 物件擷取事實資訊的元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-633">The component that retrieves the fact information from the various FactRetriever objects.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-634">failover transport (容錯移轉傳輸)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-634">failover transport</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-635">一種次要傳輸。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-635">A secondary transport.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-636">fallback trading partner agreement (後援交易夥伴協議)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-636">fallback trading partner agreement</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-637">在沒有明確協議的情況下，BizTalk Server 用於處理 B2B 訊息的設定集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-637">A collection of settings that BizTalk Server uses for business-to-business message handling, when no explicit agreement is present.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-638">File adapter (FILE 配接器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-638">File adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-639">可從檔案系統讀取訊息然後傳送到伺服器的配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-639">An adapter that can read messages from the file system and submits them to the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-640">FILE 配接器也會將伺服器傳來的訊息寫入檔案系統上的檔案中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-640">The file adapter also writes messages from the server to a file on the file system.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-641">Filter Expression property (篩選條件運算式屬性)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-641">Filter Expression property</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-642">決定可以接收哪些訊息的接收圖形的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-642">A property of a Receive shape that determines which messages can be received.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-643">接收圖形必須將啟動屬性設定為真才能具有篩選條件運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-643">The Receive shape must have the Activate property set to True to have a filter expression.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-644">Find Message view (尋找訊息檢視)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-644">Find Message view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-645">讓使用者根據追蹤的訊息屬性尋找訊息的報告檢視。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-645">A reporting view that enables users to find messages based on tracked message properties.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-646">FTP 配接器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-646">FTP adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-647">能夠在 BizTalk Server 與 FTP 伺服器之間交換檔案的配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-647">An adapter that enables exchange of files between BizTalk Server and FTP servers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-648">函數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-648">function</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-649">用來存取動作和述詞定義兩者中類別成員的抽象概念。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-649">An abstraction that is used to access class members in both the action and predicate definitions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-650">函式用於動作中，而且做為述詞中的詞彙。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-650">A function is used in actions and as a term in a predicate.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-651">functoid (運算質)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-651">functoid</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-652">執行特定計算或資料操作的可執行模組，建構 BizTalk Server 對應時以圖形方式使用，以自身為 XSLT 隨附的更豐富資訊提供基礎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-652">An executable module that performs a specific calculation or data manipulation, and that is used graphically when constructing BizTalk Server maps to provide the basis for richer transformations than what is provided by XSLT on its own.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-653">運算質 IntelliSense</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-653">Functoid IntelliSense</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-654">一項 BizTalk 對應工具功能，當運算質組態有錯誤時，此功能會在格線表面上提供視覺提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-654">A BizTalk Mapper functionality in which visual cues are provided on the grid surface, when there are errors in functoid configuration.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-655">functoid toolbox (運算質工具箱)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-655">functoid toolbox</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-656">Visual Studio 中的可停駐視窗，做為對應建構期間可用之運算質的工具板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-656">A dockable window in Visual Studio that serves as the palette of functoids available for use during map construction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-657">運算質根據其使用目的組織成不同的工具箱索引標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-657">Functoids are organized into different toolbox tabs based on their intended purpose.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-659">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-659">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-660">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-660">Definition</span></span>|

## <a name="h"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-677">H</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-677">H</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-678">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-678">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-679">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-679">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-680">handler (處理常式)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-680">handler</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-681">執行配接器的 BizTalk 主控件的執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-681">An instance of a BizTalk host on which an adapter is running.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-682">hash (雜湊)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-682">hash</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-683">對任意資料量套用單向數學函式 (有時稱為雜湊演算法) 所獲得的固定大小結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-683">A fixed-size result that is obtained by applying a one-way mathematical function (sometimes called a hash algorithm) to an arbitrary amount of data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-684">如果輸入資料有所變更，雜湊會隨之變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-684">If the input data changes, the hash changes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-685">雜湊可用於多種作業，包括驗證及數位簽章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-685">The hash can be used in many operations, including authentication and digital signing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-686">也稱為訊息摘要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-686">Also known as message digest.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-687">健康情況監控</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-687">health monitoring</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-688">監控應用程式、元件及實作 BizTalk Server 解決方案之伺服器的程序，達到預先偵側或修正問題的目的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-688">The process of monitoring applications, components, and servers on which a BizTalk Server solution is implemented for the purposes of preempting or fixing problems.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-689">Health Monitoring cube (狀況監控 Cube)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-689">Health Monitoring cube</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-690">包含訊息和服務相關資訊的線上分析處理 (OLAP) Cube。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-690">An online analytical processing (OLAP) cube that contain information about messages and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-691">BizTalk Server 隨附的兩個 Cube 為「訊息事實」與「服務事實」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-691">Two cubes included with BizTalk Server are: Message Facts and Service Facts.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-692">hierarchical view (階層檢視)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-692">hierarchical view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-693">追蹤設定檔編輯器 (TPE) 的左窗格及報告命名空間和建立 [商務活動] 檢視的區域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-693">The left pane of the Tracking Profile Editor (TPE) and the area where the reporting namespaces and Business Activity views are created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-694">主要目的在於表示追蹤設定檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-694">Its main purpose is to represent the tracking profile.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-695">History database (歷程記錄資料庫)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-695">History database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-696">「商務程序管理」實例專用的後端資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-696">A backend database specific to the Business Process Management scenario.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-697">主機</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-697">host</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-698">代表一或多個 BizTalk Server 執行階段執行個體的邏輯容器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-698">A logical container representing one or more BizTalk Server run-time instances.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-699">這是成品相關資訊駐留的程序空間 (包括所有駐留在主控件內的協調流程、結構描述、接收位置和配接器等成品)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-699">This is the process space within which information about artifacts resides (that is, all the orchestrations, schemas, receive locations, and adapters that reside within a host).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-700">主控件也做為 Windows 內的安全性網域 - 它代表主控件執行個體在一或多個伺服器上執行的虛擬程序邊界。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-700">The host also serves as a security domain within Windows - it represents a virtual process boundary within which host instances run on one or more servers.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-701">host instance (主控件執行個體)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-701">host instance</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-702">Windows NT 服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-702">A Windows NT Service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-703">主控件執行個體是特定伺服器上主控件的實體表示法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-703">A host instance is the physical representation of a host on a specific server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-704">host instance– level setting ( 主控件執行個體層級設定)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-704">host instance–level setting</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-705">BizTalk 系統管理員可以在 [BizTalk 設定儀表板] 中修改的其中一項設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-705">One of the settings that BizTalk administrators can modify in the BizTalk Settings Dashboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-706">其範例包括與協調流程記憶體節流有關的 .NET CLR 設定和屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-706">Examples include .NET CLR settings and properties related to an orchestration memory throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-707">主控件層級設定為一個主控件執行個體所專屬，基本上用於控管電腦資源 (如 RAM 或 I/O) 的使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-707">Specific to a given host instance, host-level settings essentially govern the use of a computer's resources (such as RAM or I/O).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-708">例如，最大值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-708">An example is Max.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-709">I/O 執行緒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-709">I/O Threads.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-710">host-level setting (主控件層級設定)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-710">host-level setting</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-711">BizTalk 系統管理員可以在 [BizTalk 設定儀表板] 中修改的其中一項設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-711">One of the settings that BizTalk administrators can modify in the BizTalk Settings Dashboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-712">其範例包括主控件追蹤，以及與資源型節流、速率型節流和協調流程節流相關的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-712">Examples include host tracking, and properties related to resource-based throttling, rate-based throttling, and orchestration throttling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-713">主控件層級設定可調整主控件的所有執行個體在某個部署中的行為方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-713">Host-level settings tweak the way all instances of host behave in a given deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-714">例如，若 Host1 設定最大值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-714">For example, if for Host1 the setting Max.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-715">引擎執行緒變更為 200，Host1 的所有執行個體將會使用最多 200 個引擎執行緒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-715">engine threads is changed to 200, all instances of Host1 will work with a maximum of 200 engine threads.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-716">host load balancing (主控件負載平衡)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-716">host load balancing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-717">指將多個執行 BizTalk Server 的伺服器加入至 BizTalk 群組，然後將內含式主控件的多個執行個體設定為在這些伺服器上執行的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-717">The process of adding multiple servers running BizTalk Server to a BizTalk group and then configuring multiple instances of an in-process host to run on these servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-718">這樣可將該主控件中所設定的服務和成品執行作業分散於該主控件的多個執行個體，以提高可用性和擴充性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-718">This distributes the execution of services and artifacts configured in that host across multiple instances of the host, which enhances its availability and scalability.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-719">host type (主控件類型)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-719">host type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-720">決定主控件是在 BizTalk Server 程序內或外部加以控制的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-720">A property that determines whether the host is controlled within or outside of the BizTalk Server process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-721">主控件類型為「內含式」或「外掛式」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-721">Host types are In-process or Isolated.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-722">HTTP 配接器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-722">HTTP adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-723">可以在 BizTalk Server 與任何使用 HTTP 或 HTTPS 通訊協定的應用程式之間交換訊息的配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-723">An adapter that enables exchange of messages between BizTalk Server and any application using the HTTP or HTTPS protocol.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="i"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-724">I</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-724">I</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-725">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-725">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-726">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-726">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-727">IDE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-727">IDE</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-728">請參閱 Integrated Development Environment (整合式開發環境)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-728">See Integrated Development Environment.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-729">Import/export (匯入/匯出)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-729">Import/export</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-730">在 [BizTalk 設定儀表板] 中，用於匯入/匯出設定和繫結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-730">In BizTalk Settings Dashboard, to import/export settings and bindings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-731">群組、主控件和主控件執行個體目前的 BizTalk 設定會匯出並儲存為 XML 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-731">The current BizTalk settings for group, host, and host instance are exported and saved as an XML file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-732">BizTalk 系統管理員會匯入這些設定，以將這些設定套用至其他 BizTalk 環境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-732">BizTalk administrators import these settings to apply them to another BizTalk environment.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-733">Import Wizard (匯入精靈)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-733">Import Wizard</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-734">從 BizTalk 管理主控台啟動的精靈，用於從 MSI 檔案匯入資源至 BizTalk 應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-734">A wizard that you start from the BizTalk Administration Console to import resources from an MSI file into a BizTalk application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-735">如果指定的應用程式不存在，匯入精靈將自動予以建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-735">If the specified application does not exist, the Import Wizard automatically creates it.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-736">independent composition (獨立撰寫)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-736">independent composition</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-737">兩個動作的序列，其中第二個動作開始處理商務邏輯前不依靠第一個動作的同步訊息；第二個動作可以立即開始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-737">The sequencing of two actions where the second action does not depend on a sync message from the first action before the second action begins processing business logic; the second action can begin immediately.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-738">infotip</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-738">infotip</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-739">在 Web 檢視中，以及在使用 [詳細資料] 檢視時的 [Windows 檔案總管] 的 [註解] 欄中，用來提供桌面、視窗和 [開始] 功能表命令之說明的工具提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-739">A tooltip used to provide a description for desktop, window, and Start menu commands, in Web views, and in the Windows Explorer Comment column when Details view is used.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-740">inheriting (繼承)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-740">inheriting</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-741">在交易夥伴管理 (TPM) Web 服務中，成員設定檔將繼續其父群組所有喜好設定的概念。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-741">In the Trading Partner Management (TPM) Web service, the concept that a member profile will inherit all the preferences of its parent group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-742">在非繼承群組的情況中，成員設定檔不會從父群組繼承任何喜好設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-742">In the case of a non-inheriting group, the member profile does not inherit any preferences from the parent group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-743">非繼承群組可以變更為繼承群組，但繼承群組不能變更為非繼承群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-743">A non-inheriting group can be changed to an inheriting group; however, an inheriting group cannot be changed to non-inheriting group.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-744">interruptible orchestration (可中斷協調流程)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-744">initerruptible orchestration</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-745">在程序中途妥善定義的位置點可中斷的協調流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-745">An orchestration that can be interrupted in mid-process at well-defined points.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-746">In-process host (內含式主控件)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-746">In-process host</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-747">在 BizTalk Server 程序空間內操作的主控件類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-747">A host type that operates within the BizTalk Server process space.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-748">任何協調流程可以登錄到內含式主控件，也可以由其裝載任何傳送處理常式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-748">Any orchestration can be enlisted to an In-process host, and any send handler can be hosted by it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-749">內含式主控件只能裝載內含式主控件的接收處理常式 (FILE 配接器)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-749">In-process hosts can only host receive handlers for In-process hosts (File adapter).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-750">In-process receive adapter (內含式接收配接器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-750">In-process receive adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-751">裝載於 BizTalk Server 程序內的配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-751">An adapter that is hosted in the BizTalk Server processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-752">它是由伺服器程序建立、控制和摧毀的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-752">It is created, controlled, and destroyed by server processes.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-753">安裝精靈</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-753">Installation Wizard</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-754">在匯入精靈的最後步驟啟動的精靈，用於安裝 BizTalk 應用程式到本機電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-754">A wizard that you can start during the final step of the Import Wizard to install a BizTalk application on the local computer.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-755">instance activity (執行個體活動)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-755">instance activity</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-756">一系列連續的處理步驟，其中會有一或多個訊息流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-756">A series of contiguous processing steps through which one or more messages flow.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-757">instance message (執行個體訊息)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-757">instance message</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-758">經過 BizTalk Server 的執行階段資料的不連續單位，通常表示特定商務文件 (如訂購單)，而且與定義其結構的 BizTalk Server 結構描述區別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-758">A discrete unit of run-time data flowing through BizTalk Server, usually representing a particular business document such as a purchase order, and as differentiated from the BizTalk Server schema that defines its structure.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-759">Integrated Development Environment (IDE) (整合式開發環境)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-759">Integrated Development Environment (IDE)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-760">與 Microsoft Windows 相容的使用者介面 (UI) 工具的結合組集，用來繫結、測試和改善平台及其功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-760">A combined set of Microsoft Windows-based user interface (UI) tools for building, testing, and refining a platform and its features.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-761">interceptor (攔截器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-761">interceptor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-762">從正在處理的資料流擷取資料並將資料保存到儲存區的機制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-762">A mechanism used to extract data from processing streams and persist the data to storage.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-763">interchange (交換)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-763">interchange</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-764">在 EDI 中文件的邏輯結合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-764">In EDI, a logical combination of documents.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-765">交換預定給單一收件者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-765">Interchanges are destined for a single recipient.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-766">在 BizTalk 傳訊中，交換是由接收管線的解譯階段或傳送管線的組譯階段所處理的資料內文。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-766">In BizTalk messaging, an interchange is a body of data that is processed by the disassembly stage of a receive pipeline or the assembly stage of a send pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-767">交換包含零或多個訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-767">The interchange contains zero or more messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-768">接收管線上的解譯器會從收到的交換中擷取訊息，並進一步傳播這些訊息到接收管線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-768">In a receive pipeline, the disassembler extracts the messages contained in the interchange it received, and propagates these messages further down the receive pipeline.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-769">interchange header (交換標頭)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-769">interchange header</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-770">在 EDI 中，交換的一部分或邏輯關聯文件的群組，用來指示交換的開頭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-770">In EDI, a part of an interchange, or group of logically associated documents, used to indicate the start of the interchange.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-771">interchange trailer (交換結尾)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-771">interchange trailer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-772">在 EDI 中，交換的一部分或邏輯關聯文件的群組，用來指示交換的結束。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-772">In EDI, a part of an interchange, or group of logically associated documents, used to indicate the end of the interchange.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-773">intergroup adapter (群組間配接器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-773">intergroup adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-774">在不需仰賴中繼存放區的情況下，促成兩個 BizTalk Server 群組間內部網路/區域網路通訊的 BizTalk Server 配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-774">A BizTalk Server adapter that targets intranet/LAN communication between two BizTalk Server groups without requiring intermediate storage.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-775">internal message format (內部訊息格式)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-775">internal message format</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-776">由 BizTalk Server 處理之後或之前的訊息格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-776">The format of the message after or before it is processed by BizTalk Server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-777">例如，BizTalk Server 在接收管線開始時收到的訊息是外部格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-777">For example, BizTalk Server receives a message, at the start of the receive pipeline, in the external format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-778">訊息通過管線後，就成為內部格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-778">After the message goes through the pipeline, it is in the internal format.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-779">Isolated host (外掛式主控件)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-779">Isolated host</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-780">在 BizTalk Server 安裝外操作的主控件類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-780">A host type that operates outside of the BizTalk Server installation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-781">外掛式主控件不能在其中登錄協調流程、裝載傳送處理常式、使用主控件追蹤，或做為群組的預設主控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-781">An Isolated host cannot have orchestrations enlisted to it, host a send handler, use host tracking, or be used as the default host for the group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-782">只有外掛式主控件的接收處理常式 (HTTP、SOAP) 可以由外掛式主控件裝載。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-782">Only those receive handlers for Isolated hosts (HTTP, SOAP) can be hosted by an Isolated host.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-783">isolated receive adapter (外掛式接收配接器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-783">isolated receive adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-784">裝載在 BizTalk Server 程序之外其他程序中的接收配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-784">The receive adapter that is hosted in a process other than a BizTalk Server process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-785">此配接器由外部程序建立及控制，而且在執行階段與 BizTalk Server 一起註冊以提交訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-785">This adapter is created and controlled by external process and it registers with BizTalk server at run time to submit messages.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-787">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-787">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-788">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-788">Definition</span></span>|
