|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-789">關鍵效能指標 (KPI)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-789">Key Performance Indicator (KPI)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-790">Analysis Services 提供的可自訂商務計量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-790">Customizable business metrics provided by Analysis Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-791">KPI 由相關的屬性以及產生產業標準目標和基準線的關聯計算組成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-791">KPIs consist of relevant attributes and associated calculations that generate industry-standard goals and benchmarks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-792">KPI 集合包含量值、目標、顯示屬性和變異。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-792">A KPI collection includes a measure, a goal, display properties, and variances.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-793">公司使用 KPI 追蹤效能並改善制定決策的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-793">Companies use KPIs to track performance and improve decision-making abilities.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="l"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-794">L</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-794">L</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-795">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-795">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-796">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-796">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-797">late bound port (晚期繫結連接埠)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-797">late bound port</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-798">協調流程中定義的連接埠，其「繫結」屬性設定為「稍後指定」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-798">A port defined in the orchestration, which has the Binding property set to Specify later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-799">晚期繫結連接埠是在繫結到實體連接埠時才設定組態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-799">A late bound port is configured when it is bound to a physical port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-800">使用 BizTalk 管理主控台可以執行繫結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-800">The binding is performed using the    BizTalk Administration Console.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-801">line-of-business application (商業實務應用程式)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-801">line-of-business application</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-802">對經營企業很重要的應用程式，如薪水、資源規畫、供應鏈管理和會計。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-802">An application that is vital to running enterprises, such as payroll, resource planning, supply chain management, and accounting.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-803">live data (即時資料)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-803">live data</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-804">目前由 BizTalk Server 進行處理的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-804">Data that is currently being processed by BizTalk Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-805">locally unique identifier (LUID) (本機唯一識別碼)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-805">locally unique identifier (LUID)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-806">在 BizTalk 群組中用於唯一識別成品的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-806">A name for an artifact that identifies it uniquely in the BizTalk group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-807">視成品類型而定，LUID 的組成項目將有所不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-807">The elements comprising the LUID may vary, depending on the type of artifact.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-808">例如，BizTalk 組件的 LUID 包含其名稱、版本、文化特性和公開金鑰 Token，像是 Microsoft.BizTalk.Hws.HwsPromotedProperties, Version=3.0.1.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-808">For example, the LUID for a BizTalk assembly includes its name, version, culture, and public key token, such as Microsoft.BizTalk.Hws.HwsPromotedProperties, Version=3.0.1.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-809">long-running transaction (長時間執行的交易)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-809">long-running transaction</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-810">視為一個單位的動作集合，通常以堅固和可預測的形式維護適當狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-810">A collection of actions treated as a unit, typically used to maintain an appropriate state in a robust and predictable fashion.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-811">交易可以在無限期的時間內發生，並包含數個巢狀交易。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-811">The transaction can take place over an indefinite period of time and contain several nested transactions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-812">looping record (迴圈記錄)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-812">looping record</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-813">一個執行個體訊息可以有多個相符項目的結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-813">A structure that can have more than one occurrence in an instance message.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="m"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-814">M</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-814">M</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-815">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-815">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-816">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-816">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-817">管理資料庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-817">Management database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-818">儲存組態資訊做為組織資源的 Microsoft SQL Server 資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-818">A Microsoft SQL Server database that stores the configuration information for resources in an organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-819">每個組織各有一個管理資料庫 (有時稱為組態資料庫)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-819">There is one Management database (sometimes referred to as the configuration database) per organization.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-820">地圖 (map)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-820">map</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-821">在一規格中的記錄和欄位以及其他規格中的記錄和欄位之間，定義對應關係的 XML 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-821">An XML file that defines the correspondence between the records and fields in one specification and the records and fields in another specification.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-822">對應包含 Extensible Stylesheet Language (XSL) 樣式表，BizTalk Server 使用此樣式表執行對應中描述的轉換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-822">A map contains an Extensible Stylesheet Language (XSL) stylesheet that is used by BizTalk Server to perform the transformation described in the map.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-823">mapper grid (對應工具方格)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-823">mapper grid</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-824">BizTalk Mapper 主視窗的多層中間區域，介於來源和目的結構描述之間，在其中定義資料對應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-824">The multi-layered middle area of the main BizTalk Mapper window, between the source and destination schemas, in which data mapping is defined.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-825">mapper grid page (對應工具格線頁面)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-825">mapper grid page</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-826">對應工具方格的單一層，用來組織與其他資料對應分開的相關資料對應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-826">A single layer in the mapper grid, used to organize related data mappings separate from other data mappings.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-827">master secret (主要密碼)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-827">master secret</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-828">在企業單一登入 (SSO) 管理員要求時由主要密碼伺服器產生的金鑰。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-828">A key generated by the master secret server when an Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO) Administrator requests it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-829">此密碼金鑰儲存於登錄，做為主要密碼伺服器上的 Local Security Authority (LSA) 密碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-829">This secret key is stored in the registry as a Local Security Authority (LSA) secret on the master secret server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-830">只有 SSO 管理員可以存取此密碼金鑰。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-830">Only SSO Administrators can access this secret key.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-831">master secret server (主要密碼伺服器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-831">master secret server</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-832">在分散式企業單一登入 (SSO) 環境，登錄中儲存主要密碼金鑰的一台電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-832">In a distributed Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO) environment, the one computer that holds the master secret key in the registry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-833">可以有許多 SSO 伺服器 (不同電腦) 存取此單一 SSO 資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-833">There can be many SSO servers (on different machines) accessing this single SSO database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-834">其中一個 SSO 伺服器是專門當成主要密碼伺服器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-834">Only one of these SSO servers is designated to be the master secret server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-835">message</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-835">message</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-836">資料的電子執行個體，通常在兩個執行的商務程序或應用程式之間進行交換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-836">An electronic instance of data, as typically exchanged between two running business processes or applications.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-837">message body part (訊息內文部分)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-837">message body part</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-838">BizTalk Server 訊息的主要部分，包含實際內容，且大部分時候會包含 XML BLOB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-838">The main part of a BizTalk Server message, which contains the actual payload, and in most cases an XML blob.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-839">所有訊息最多只能有一個內文部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-839">All messages must have at most one body part.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-840">一般來說，從對應到 BizTalk Server 訊息內文部分讀取的資料會用來升級訊息內容屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-840">Typically the data read from the stream corresponding to the BizTalk Server message body part is used for promoting message context properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-841">因此根據升級屬性的路由、發佈或訂閱通常都是以內文部分來完成的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-841">Hence the routing, publication, or subscription that is based on promoted properties is generally done based on the body part.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-842">message context (訊息內容)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-842">message context</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-843">BizTalk Server 處理文件時使用的各種屬性之容器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-843">A container for various properties that are used by BizTalk Server when processing a document.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-844">訊息內容屬性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-844">message context properties</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-845">與訊息相關的一組屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-845">A set of properties associated with the message.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-846">Message Details view (訊息詳細資料檢視)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-846">Message Details view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-847">在 [群組中樞] 頁面上，MessageBox 中某個訊息的所有已知資訊的詳細檢視。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-847">On the Group Hub page, a detailed view of all known information for a given message in the MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-848">透過兩種 [作業] 檢視之一，從樞紐分析表欄位清單的快顯功能表可存取此檢視。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-848">This view is available through the shortcut menu in the PivotTable field list in one of two Operations views.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-849">message digest (訊息摘要)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-849">message digest</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-850">請參閱＜其他詞彙：hash (雜湊)＞</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-850">See Other Term: hash</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-851">Message Facts cube (訊息事實 Cube)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-851">Message Facts cube</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-852">彙總訊息和服務相關資訊的線上分析處理 (OLAP) Cube。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-852">An online analytical processing (OLAP) cube that aggregates information about messages and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-853">現成提供的兩個 Cube 包括「訊息事實」與「服務事實」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-853">Two cubes included out of the box are: Message Facts and Service Facts.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-854">訊息流程</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-854">message flow</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-855">一系列連續的處理步驟，其中會有一或多個訊息流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-855">A series of contiguous processing steps through which one or more messages flow.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-856">Message Flow view (訊息流程檢視)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-856">Message Flow view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-857">「群組中樞」頁面上的一種檢視，可顯示特定訊息的處理事件歷程記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-857">A view on the Group Hub page that displays a history of processing events for specific messages.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-858">message header (訊息標頭)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-858">message header</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-859">在 EDI 中，用來指示文件開頭的訊息部分，是邏輯結合區段的集結，其中包含一個交易的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-859">In EDI, a part of the message used to indicate the start of a document, which is a bundle of logically combined segments containing information about one transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-860">在 ANSI X.12 中，訊息等同於交易集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-860">In ANSI X.12, a message is equivalent to a transaction set.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-861">message instance (訊息執行個體)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-861">message instance</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-862">BizTalk Server 正在處理，或已序列化至 MessageBox 或追蹤資料存放區以分別做進一步處理或追蹤之訊息的執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-862">An instance of a message that BizTalk Server is either processing or has serialized into the MessageBox or Tracking datastore for further processing or tracking, respectively.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-863">在 BizTalk Server 內，這通常是訊息的參考、訊息的升級屬性以及訊息內文。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-863">Within BizTalk Server, this is usually a reference to the message, the promoted properties of the message, and the message body.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-864">Message Metrics view (訊息計量檢視)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-864">Message Metrics view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-865">訊息計量線上分析處理 (OLAP) Cube 的樞紐分析表檢視。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-865">The PivotTableview into a message metrics online analytical processing (OLAP) cube.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-866">message trailer (訊息結尾)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-866">message trailer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-867">在 EDI 中，用來指示文件結束的訊息部分，是邏輯結合區段的集結，其中包含一個交易的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-867">In EDI, a part of the message used to indicate the end of a document, which is a bundle of logically combined segments containing information about one transaction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-868">在 ANSI X.12 中，訊息等同於交易集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-868">In ANSI X.12, a message is equivalent to a transaction set.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-869">MessageBox binding (MessageBox 繫結)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-869">MessageBox binding</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-870">與 MessageBox 互動的繫結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-870">A binding that interacts with the MessageBox.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-875">Messages view (訊息檢視)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-875">Messages view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-876">在「群組中樞」頁面上，MessageBox 中服務使用的訊息執行個體的即時檢視。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-876">On the Group Hub page, a live view of message instances used by services in a MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-877">此檢視在 [作業] 功能表可以取得。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-877">The view is available in the Operations menu.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-878">Messaging (傳訊)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-878">Messaging</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-879">BizTalk Server 的主要功能之一，促成可靠的訊息接收、路由與散佈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-879">One of the primary functions of BizTalk Server, involving the reliable reception, routing and distribution of messages.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-888">mixed content (混合內容)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-888">mixed content</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-889">特定 XML 項目的內容，同時包含子項目以及不在子項目內的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-889">The content of a particular XML element that contains both subelements and data that is not within the subelements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-890">HTML 的範例是︰ &lt;P&gt;共 &lt;EM&gt;一律&lt;/e m&gt; 日落，增加或減少上升。&lt;/ P&gt;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-890">An example from HTML is: &lt;P&gt;Full moons &lt;EM&gt;always&lt;/EM&gt; rise at sunset, more or less.&lt;/P&gt;</span></span>|

## <a name="p"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-934">P</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-934">P</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-935">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-935">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-936">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-936">Definition</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-937">PAM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-937">PAM</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-938">請參閱 Partner Agreement Management (PAM) (夥伴協議管理)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-938">See Partner Agreement Management (PAM).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-939">參數 (parameter)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-939">parameter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-940">指商務程序的預設參數、每個夥伴的商務程序參數，以及每個夥伴群組的商務程序參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-940">Refers to the default parameters of a business process, parameters for a business process per partner, and parameters for a business process per partner group.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-941">夥伴</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-941">partner</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-942">請參閱＜其他詞彙：trading partner (交易夥伴)＞</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-942">See Other Term: trading partner</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-943">Partner Agreement Management (PAM) (夥伴協議管理)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-943">Partner Agreement Management (PAM)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-944">在 BizTalk Server 管理主控台的 [合作對象] 節點中，用來設定合作對象屬性的使用者介面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-944">A user interface in the Parties node of the BizTalk Server Administration Console where you set party properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-945">您可以設定從事 EDI 文件交換、EDI 批次處理和 AS2 文件傳輸之合作對象的處理屬性，以及當合作對象不存在時所使用的全域屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-945">You can set processing properties for parties engaging in EDI document exchange, EDI batching, AS2 document transport, and global properties to be used in the absence of a party.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-946">party (合作對象)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-946">party</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-947">BizTalk Server 外部與協調流程互動的每個實體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-947">Each entity outside of BizTalk Server that interacts with an orchestration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-948">與貴組織合作的所有夥伴皆視為合作對象，而且貴組織可能有數千個合作對象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-948">All of the partners your organization deals with are considered parties, and your organization may have several has several thousands partners.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-949">party enlistment (合作對象登錄)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-949">party enlistment</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-950">繫結合作對象到角色的機制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-950">The mechanism that ties a party to a role.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-951">您可以在角色中登錄合作對象，因而讓協調流程能夠與合作對象互動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-951">You can enlist a party in a role, and that enables the orchestration to interact with the party</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-952">pass-through (通過)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-952">pass-through</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-953">BizTalk Server 連接埠的組態，在傳送埠上僅使用一個篩選條件運算式，將接收埠直接連接到傳送埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-953">A configuration of BizTalk Server ports such that a receive port is directly connected to a send port by using only one filter expression on a send port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-954">篩選條件運算式的格式應該為 BTS.ReceivePortName == "名稱或接收埠"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-954">The filter expression should take the form BTS.ReceivePortName == "Name or receive port".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-955">在這種組態中，接收埠接收的任何訊息會直接傳送到傳送埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-955">In this configuration, any message that is received by the receive port is directly routed to a send port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-956">BizTalk 2004 中通過執行的意義與 BizTalk Server 2000 或 2002年中通過執行的意義不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-956">The meaning of pass-through execution in BizTalk 2004 is different from the meaning of pass-through execution in BizTalk Server 2000 or 2002.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-957">在 BizTalk Server 2004 中通過執行訊息仍在管線中處理，並可能在連接埠數目也會進行轉換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-957">In BizTalk Server 2004, the pass-through execution message is still processed in pipelines and may be transformed in ports as well.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-958">效能監視</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-958">performance monitoring</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-959">觀看訊息程序/接收速率、執行協調流程數、快取點擊數、一段時間的記憶使用狀況等的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-959">The process of watching the message process/receive rate, number of running orchestrations, number of cache hits, memory usage over time, and so on.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-960">performance processing rules (效能處理規則)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-960">performance processing rules</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-961">管理程序效能或容量類型計數器的規則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-961">Rules that govern process performance or capacity type counters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-962">周邊網路</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-962">perimeter network</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-963">位於內部網路與網際網路之間的裝置和子網路的集合，可隔離未獲授權的網際網路使用者，以協助保護內部網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-963">A collection of devices and subnets placed between an intranet and the Internet to help protect the intranet from unauthorized Internet users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-964">也稱為 DMZ 以及過濾的子網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-964">Also known as DMZ, demilitarized zone, and screened subnet.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-965">physical (early) binding (實體早期繫結)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-965">physical (early) binding</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-966">做為組件中一部分的資訊，由部署程序使用來建立傳送埠和接收埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-966">Information that is carried in the assembly and used by the deployment process to create send and receive ports.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-967">pipeline (管線)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-967">pipeline</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-968">定義及連結一或多個處理階段的軟體基礎結構，以指定的順序執行來完成特定工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-968">A software infrastructure that defines and links one or more processing stages, running them in prescribed order to complete a specific task.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-969">管理將處理分成各個階段，描述工作類別的抽象概念。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-969">Pipelines divide processing into stages, abstractions that describe a category of work.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-970">它也決定執行每個工作類別的順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-970">They also determine the sequence in which each category of work is performed.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-971">pipeline component (管線元件)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-971">pipeline component</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-972">COM 或 .NET 相容元件，可放置在管線中，在訊息經過該管線時執行一些處理動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-972">A COM or .NET-based component that can be placed into a pipeline to perform some processing action on the messages going through that pipeline.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-973">管線設計師</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-973">Pipeline Designer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-974">用來建立和設定 BizTalk Server 中管線的圖形使用者介面工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-974">A graphical user-interface tool used to create and configure pipelines in BizTalk Server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-975">policy (原則)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-975">policy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-976">各種版本的商務規則集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-976">A versioned collection of business rules.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-977">port connector line (連接埠連接線)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-977">port connector line</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-978">顯示傳送/接收圖形與連接埠圖形上作業之間的連接線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-978">A line showing the connection between a Send/Receive shape and an operation on a Port shape.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-979">連接埠連接線的結束點都不能保持為未連接狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-979">Neither endpoint of a port connector line can remain unattached.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-980">port type (連接埠類型)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-980">port type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-981">定義該結束點允許之訊息互動模式組合 (稱為作業) 的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-981">A property that defines the set of message interaction patterns called operations that are permitted at that endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-982">作業可以是單向，其中傳送或接收一個訊息，或者可以是要求-回應，其中會傳送 (或接收) 訊息並接收 (或傳送) 回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-982">An operation can be one-way, in which case one message is sent or received, or it could be request-response in which case a message is sent (or received) and a response is received (or sent).</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-983">positional flat file (位置一般檔案)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-983">positional flat file</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-984">用來表示商務文件的檔案格式類型，其中記錄和欄位有固定長度，因為不需要加隔符號。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-984">A type of file format used to represent business documents in which the records and fields have a fixed length, eliminating the need for delimiters.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-985">private queue (私用佇列)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-985">private queue</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-986">不是發佈為 Active Directory 物件的佇列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-986">A queue that is not published as an Active Directory object.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-987">BizTalk 訊息佇列完全支援在私用佇列中訊息的傳送和接收。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-987">BizTalk message queuing fully supports the sending and receiving of messages into private queues.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-988">process surface (程序介面)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-988">process surface</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-989">協調流程設計師中設計介面的中間區域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-989">The middle area of the design surface in the Orchestration Designer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-990">這個區域用來設計協調流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-990">This area is used to design orchestrations.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-991">Project Designer (專案設計師)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-991">Project Designer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-992">組成專案的服務、連接埠和繫結的視覺表示法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-992">A visual representation of the services, ports, and bindings that make up a project.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-993">新增和移除服務、建立和移除設計師內服務上相容連接埠之間的繫結，使用者即可在專案設計師中編輯視覺項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-993">Users can edit the visual items in the Project Designer by adding and removing services, and creating and removing bindings between compatible ports on the services in the designer.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-994">property promotion (屬性升級)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-994">property promotion</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-995">透過此特定的訊息屬性寫入訊息內容與訊息相關聯，做為屬性欄位機制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-995">The mechanism through which specific message properties are written to the message context associated with the message as property fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-996">寫入至訊息內容屬性欄位會被視為已提升的屬性的屬性 ( **IsPromoted** 欄位的屬性設定為 **True**)，而且需要相關聯的屬性結構描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-996">Properties written to the message context as property fields are considered to be promoted properties (the **IsPromoted** property of the field is set to **True**) and require an associated property schema.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="cc989-997">BizTalk Server 傳訊引擎的文件追蹤的訊息路由的指南，用於評估協調流程中使用屬性欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-997">Property fields are used by the BizTalk Server Messaging Engine for purposes of document routing, message tracking, and for evaluation in orchestrations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-998">訊息的訊息內容會儲存在 MessageBox 資料庫的多工緩衝處理表格中，該訊息所在資料列的 imgContext 一欄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-998">The message context for a message is stored in the imgContext column of the row for the message in the spool table of the MessageBox database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-999">屬性結構描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-999">property schema</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1000">與 BizTalk Server 結構描述關聯的結構描述，用於識別文件中即將升級至訊息內容做為屬性欄位的項目欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1000">A schema that you associate with a BizTalk Server schema, and used to identify the element fields in a document that will be promoted to the message context as property fields.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1001">protocol setting (通訊協定設定)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1001">protocol setting</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1002">此設定定義使用特定 B2B 通訊協定來支援商務交易的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1002">A setting that defines how business transactions are to be supported for a specific business-to-business protocol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1003">每個商務設定檔都會針對夥伴可用於通訊的每個 B2B 通訊協定來定義各種設定，以便處理訊息 (編碼) 或傳送訊息 (傳輸)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1003">Each business profile defines the various settings for processing messages (encoding) or transmitting messages (transport) for each of the business-to-business protocols over which the partner can communicate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1004">通訊協定設定可適用於編碼通訊協定或傳輸通訊協定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1004">A protocol setting can be for encoding protocols or for a transport protocol.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1005">public queue (公用佇列)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1005">public queue</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1006">發佈為 Active Directory 物件的佇列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1006">A queue that is published as an Active Directory object.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1007">publication-subscription (發佈-訂閱)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1007">publication-subscription</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1008">請參閱＜其他詞彙：publish/subscribe architecture (發佈/訂閱架構)＞</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1008">See Other Term: publish/subscribe architecture</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1009">publish/subscribe architecture (發佈/訂閱架構)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1009">publish/subscribe architecture</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1010">發佈與訂閱的組合，用於在子系統之間移動訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1010">The combination of publication and subscription used  to move messages between subsystems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1011">例如，接收埠接收訊息、處理訊息，然後發佈訊息至 MessageBox。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1011">For example, receive ports receive messages, process them and  publish them to the MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1012">BizTalk Server 將這些訊息路由至進一步處理文件的訂閱協調流程或傳送埠，然後重新發佈至 MessageBox 或傳送到外部系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1012">BizTalk Server routes these messages to subscribing orchestrations or send ports that further process the documents and either republish them to the MessageBox or send them to external systems.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1013">發行</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1013">publishing</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1014">將訊息執行個體儲存到 MessageBox 資料庫的動作，因此可與取用應用程式中的訂閱比對。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1014">The act of storing a message instance in the MessageBox database so that it can be matched to a subscription from a consuming application.</span></span>|

## <a name="r"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-1020">R</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1020">R</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1021">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1021">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1022">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1022">Definition</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1023">range dimension (範圍維度)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1023">range dimension</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1024">在 BAM 中，用來建立準則範圍的維度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1024">In BAM, a dimension used to create ranges of crirteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1025">例如，您可以建立「低」(0-100)、「中」(100-500) 和「高」(500-1000) 三種範圍來描述銷售額的數值範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1025">For example, you could create Low (0-100), Medium (100-500), and High (500-1000) ranges to describe sales of numerical units.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1026">receipt generator (回條產生器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1026">receipt generator</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1027">產生假回條的元件，以從重試佇列移除訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1027">A component that generates a fake receipt to remove a message from the Retry Queue.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1028">如果傳訊埠設定要使用可靠傳訊，則會使用此元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1028">This component is used if a messaging port is configured to use Reliable Messaging.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1029">receive handler (接收處理常式)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1029">receive handler</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1030">執行接收配接器的 BizTalk 主控件的執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1030">An instance of a BizTalk host on which a receive adapter is running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1031">接收處理常式是待命程式元件、結束點管理員元件和 MessageAgent 元件的邏輯容器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1031">A receive handler is a logical container for a Listener component, an Endpoint Manager component, and a MessageAgent component.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1032">receive handler host type (接收處理常式主控件類型)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1032">receive handler host type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1033">將主控件類型限制為可以裝載特定接收處理常式的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1033">A property that restricts the host type by which a particular receive handler can be hosted.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1034">receive location (接收位置)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1034">receive location</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1035">位置 (如 URL) 和配接器類型的實體、設計階段概念。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1035">The physical, design-time notion of a location (such as a URL) and an adapter type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1036">BizTalk Server 管理主控台中主控台節點的接收位置定義了接收功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1036">A receive location in the Host node in the BizTalk Server Administration console defines the receive functionality.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1037">receive pipeline (接收管線)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1037">receive pipeline</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1038">配接器收到訊息後發佈至 MessageBox 資料庫前，在訊息上執行的管線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1038">A pipeline that is executed on messages after they have been received by an adapter and before they are published into the MessageBox database.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1039">receive port (接收埠)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1039">receive port</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1040">相似接收位置的邏輯群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1040">A logical grouping of similar receive locations.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1041">redeploy (重新部署)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1041">redeploy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1042">刪除舊位元並部署新位元，藉以重新部署已經存在於目標環境中的組件之動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1042">The act of redeploying an assembly that already exists in the target environment by deleting the old bits and deploying the new ones.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1043">rehydrate (解除凍結)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1043">rehydrate</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1044">在某些事件發生 (如接收訊息) 時，從永久儲存區的記憶體中啟動閒置協調流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1044">To activate an idle orchestration in memory from persistent storage as a result of some event taking place, such as a message being received.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1045">相關性檢視</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1045">Relevance view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1046">BizTalk 對應工具的一種檢視，其中結構描述項目的不相關同層級項目會摺疊起來，以提供更簡潔的結構描述檢視。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1046">A view in BizTalk Mapper whereby non-relevant siblings of a schema element collapse to provide a more compact view of the schema.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1047">這樣可減少捲動需求，而將焦點放在結構描述與對應的實用部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1047">This reduces the need for scrolling, and brings the focus to the useful parts of the schema and map.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1048">Reporting views (報告檢視)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1048">Reporting vews</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1049">顯示商務程序的檢視階層集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1049">A hierarchical set of views that show a business process or processes.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1050">儲存機制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1050">repository</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1051">Analysis Services 使用的中繼資料的儲存區容器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1051">The storage container for the metadata used by Analysis Services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1052">中繼資料儲存於關聯式資料庫中的資料表，用來定義 Analysis Server 物件的參數和屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1052">Metadata is stored in tables in a relational database and is used to define the parameters and properties of Analysis server objects.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1053">XML 工具在讀-寫模式中使用儲存機制，而 BizTalk 總管以唯讀模式存取資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1053">XML tools use the repository in read-write mode, while BizTalk Explorer accesses the data in read-only mode.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1054">request-response adapter (要求-回應配接器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1054">request-response adapter</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1055">從用戶端接收要求訊息、將訊息提交到伺服器、等候回應，然後將回應傳送回用戶端的接收配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1055">A receive adapter that receives a request message from the client, submits it to the server, waits for a response, and then sends the response back to the client.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1056">Return shape (返回圖形)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1056">Return shape</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1057">在協調流程實際結束前用來在某個時間點終止協調流程的圖形。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1057">A shape used to terminate an orchestration at some point before the orchestration's true end.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1058">可能的範例：If (security check passed) continue, else Return.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1058">An example of this might be: If (security check passed) continue, else Return.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1059">角色 (role)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1059">role</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1060">使用服務或實作服務的連接埠類型之集合，提供合作對象與協調流程互動的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1060">A collection of port types that either uses a service or implements a service, providing the means by which parties interact with orchestration(s).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1061">例如，協調流程可能使用託運商的角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1061">For example, an orchestration might use the role of a Shipper.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1062">託運商可能有一或多個合作對象與它關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1062">The Shipper would have one or two parties associated with it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1063">協調流程決定要僱用哪家託運公司運送項目時，它會比較託運商角色中合作對象的價格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1063">When the orchestration decides which shipping company to use to ship an item, it compares the prices of the parties in the Shipper role.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1064">role link (角色連結)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1064">role link</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1065">角色之間的關係，藉由雙方互動時所使用的連接埠和訊息來定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1065">The relationship between roles by defined by the message and port types used in the interactions in both directions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1066">role link type (角色連結類型)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1066">role link type</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1067">定義關係中每個服務扮演的部分，以及指定每個角色提供的連接埠類型，確定兩個服務或協調流程之間關係特徵的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1067">A property that characterizes the relationship between two services or orchestrations by defining the part played by each of the services in the relationship and specifying the port types provided by each role.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1068">root node (根節點)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1068">root node</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1069">BizTalk Server 結構描述內的節點，表示結構描述所指定之商務文件中最外層的 XML 項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1069">A node within a BizTalk Server schema that represents the outermost XML element in the business document specified by the schema.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1070">RTA window (RTA 視窗)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1070">RTA window</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1071">定義即時彙總 (RTA) 中資料彙總的時間週期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1071">Defines the time period over which the data in a real-time aggregation (RTA) is aggregated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1072">例如，如果時間週期是一天，而時間點是現在，您只會看到過去 24 小時的資料彙總。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1072">For example, if the time period is one day and the point in time is now, then you see aggregations only on the data from the last 24 hours.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1073">因為時間點不斷在變更中，所以 RTA 視窗中的時間週期也會變更；因此，它也稱為移動時間視窗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1073">As the point in time is continuously changing, the time period in the RTA window is also changing; therefore, it is also referred to as a moving time window.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1074">rule (規則)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1074">rule</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1075">條件和動作的配對。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1075">A pairing of conditions and actions.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1076">rule set (規則集)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1076">rule set</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1077">相似規則的邏輯群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1077">A logical grouping of similar rules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1078">可做為規則引擎的群組/分割機制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1078">This can be viewed as a grouping/partitioning mechanism of the rule engine.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1079">Rules Engine Framework (規則引擎架構)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1079">Rules Engine Framework</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1080">應用程式開發人員使用的 .NET 元件庫、API 和服務，用來撰寫以規則為基礎的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1080">The .NET component library, APIs, and services used by application developers to write rule-based applications.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1081">Rules Engine Update service (規則引擎更新服務)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1081">Rules Engine Update service</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1082">執行動態原則更新的服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1082">A service that performs dynamic policy updates.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1083">Rules store (規則存放區)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1083">Rules store</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1084">保存原則的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1084">A location for persisting policies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1085">SQL Server 資料庫是預設的規則存放區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1085">A SQL Server database is the default rule store.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="s"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-1086">S</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1086">S</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1087">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1087">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1088">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1088">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1089">結構描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1089">schema</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1090">訊息的結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1090">The structure for a message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1091">結構描述可包含多個子結構描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1091">A schema can contain multiple sub-schema.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1092">Schema Editor extension (結構描述編輯器延伸模組)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1092">Schema Editor extension</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1093">軟體模組延伸 BizTalk 編輯器支援的基本 XML/XSD 功能的機制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1093">The mechanism through which software modules extend the basic XML/XSD functionality supported by BizTalk Editor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1094">結構描述編輯器延伸模組一般會將補充屬性新增到 BizTalk 結構描述中一或多個節點，以表示其特定語意。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1094">Schema Editor Extensions typically add supplemental properties to one or more nodes in BizTalk schemas to represent their particular semantics.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1095">過濾的子網路</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1095">screened subnet</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1096">請參閱＜其他詞彙：perimeter network (周邊網路)＞</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1096">See Other Term: perimeter network</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1097">安全通訊端層</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1097">Secure Sockets Layer</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1098">通訊協定，藉由使用資料加密、數位憑證和公開金鑰加密的組合提高資料通訊的安全性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1098">A protocol that improves the security of data communication by using a combination of data encryption, digital certificates, and public key cryptography.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1099">SSL 會啟用驗證並提升網路上的資料完整性與隱私權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1099">SSL enables authentication and increases data integrity and privacy over networks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1100">SSL 不提供授權或不可否認性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1100">SSL does not provide authorization or nonrepudiation.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1101">segment (區段)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1101">segment</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1102">在 EDI 中項目的邏輯結合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1102">In EDI, a logical combination of elements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1103">例如，名稱和地址詳細資料會結合到一個區段中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1103">For example, name and address details are combined in one segment.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1104">segment tag (區段標記)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1104">segment tag</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1105">在 EDI 中區段的唯一識別碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1105">In EDI, a unique identifier for a segment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1106">例如，在 EDIFACT 內，區段標記是三個大寫字母的代碼，做為文件內項目的前置詞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1106">Within EDIFACT, for example, segment tags are three-letter uppercase codes that prefix the elements within a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1107">在 ANSI X.12 中，區段標記是二或三個大寫字母代碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1107">In ANSI X.12, the segment tags are two or three-letter uppercase codes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1108">區段標記與記錄類型識別項類似。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1108">A segment tag is similar to a record type identifier.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1109">send handler (傳送處理常式)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1109">send handler</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1110">與傳送配接器相關聯的 BizTalk 主控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1110">A BizTalk host with which the send adapter is associated.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1111">send pipeline (傳送管線)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1111">send pipeline</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1112">訊息從 BizTalk Server 送出前，在訊息上執行的管線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1112">A pipeline that is executed on messages before they are sent out of the BizTalk server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1113">send port (傳送埠)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1113">send port</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1114">傳送訊息的目標位置或是接收訊息的位置，也是指用來實作通訊動作的技術。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1114">The location to which messages are sent or from which messages are received, and the technology that is used to implement the communication action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1115">這個位置只會由這個連接埠的名稱唯一識別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1115">The location is uniquely identified by the name of the port.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1116">send port group (傳送埠群組)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1116">send port group</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1117">傳送埠的邏輯群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1117">A logical grouping of send ports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1118">將訊息傳送至傳送埠群組時，該訊息會路由至所有相關的傳送埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1118">When a message is sent to a send port group, it is routed to all of the associated send ports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1119">也稱為通訊群組清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1119">Also referred to as a distribution list.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1120">服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1120">service</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1121">執行特定系統功能支援作業系統層級之其他程式 (如 Windows NT 服務) 的程式、常式或程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1121">A program, routine, or process that performs a specific system function to support other programs at the operating systems level, such as a Windows NT service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1122">服務是在伺服器上執行的 Windows NT 服務或 COM+ 服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1122">A service is a Windows NT service or a COM+ service that runs on a server.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1123">service instance (服務執行個體)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1123">service instance</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1124">通常是指 BizTalk Server 正在處理，或已序列化至 MessageBox 做進一步處理或追蹤之協調流程的執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1124">Generally refers to an instance of an orchestration that BizTalk Server is either processing or has serialized into the MessageBox for further processing or tracking.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1125">這通常是協調流程狀態的序列化表示法，再加上協調流程中使用之任何訊息的參考。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1125">This is usually a serialized representation of the state of the orchestration and references to any messages in use within the orchestration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1126">在傳訊過程中，服務執行個體會套用至連接埠的執行個體，例如，接收埠的輸入為接收位置而輸出為發佈至 MessageBox 資料庫，或傳送埠的輸入為 MessageBox 而輸出通常是傳送配接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1126">In the context of messaging, a service instance applies to an instance of a port, for example, a receive port where the input is the receive location and the output is publishing to the MessageBox database, or a send port where the input is the MessageBox and the output is typically a send adapter.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1127">Service Metrics view (服務計量檢視)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1127">Service Metrics view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1128">服務計量 OLAP Cube 的樞紐分析表檢視。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1128">A PivotTable view into the service metrics OLAP cube.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1129">之前屬於彙總檢視的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1129">Formerly part of Aggregation view.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1194">static port (靜態連接埠)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1194">static port</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1195">有目的位址也有關聯的配接器類型的傳送埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1195">A send port that has a destination address and adapter type associated with it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1196">與動態傳送埠意義相反，靜態傳送埠在執行階段不能變更其組態，而且永遠只能傳送訊息到一個目的位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1196">As opposed to a dynamic send port, a static send port cannot change its configuration at run time and is always used to send messages to only one destination address.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1201">submit (提交)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1201">submit</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1202">在 MessageBox 資料庫的適當資料表中放置訊息和相關屬性，及掃描訂閱目錄以尋找其述詞符合訊息屬性的訂閱之動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1202">The act of placing a message and associated properties in the appropriate tables in the MessageBox database and scanning the Subscription directory for subscriptions whose predicates match the properties of the message.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1203">subscribe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1203">subscribe</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1204">BizTalk 指示 MessageBox 將屬性符合指定參數 (訂閱) 的訊息路由至適當程序的機制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1204">A BizTalk mechanism for instructing the MessageBox to route messages with properties that meet specified parameters (subscriptions) to the appropriate processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1205">例如，傳送埠篩選條件在 MessageBox 中建立訂閱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1205">For example, send port filters create subscriptions in the MessageBox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1206">符合篩選條件規格的訊息一旦發佈至 MessageBox，BizTalk Server 便將訊息路由到訂閱的傳送埠進行處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1206">When messages are published to the MessageBox that match the filter specification, BizTalk Server routes the messages to the subscribing send port for processing.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1207">訂閱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1207">subscription</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1208">將符合特定屬性比較準則的訊息路由到工作佇列的機制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1208">A mechanism to route messages that match certain property comparison criteria into a Work queue.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1209">訂閱資料庫</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1209">Subscription database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1210">包含 MessageBox 群組所有訂閱的 MessageBox 資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1210">The MessageBox database that contains all of the subscriptions for a MessageBox group.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1211">suspended instance (擱置的執行個體)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1211">suspended instance</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1212">由於系統或訊息中有錯誤，BizTalk Server 已停止處理的訊息或協調流程的執行個體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1212">An instance of a message or orchestration that BizTalk Server has stopped processing, due to an error in the system or the message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1213">一般來說，因系統錯誤而擱置的執行個體會在系統問題獲得解決後繼續。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1213">Generally, suspended instances caused by system errors are resumable upon resolution of the system issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1214">因訊息有問題而擱置的執行個體則通常無法繼續，且必須修正訊息本身並重新提交至 BizTalk Server 系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1214">Often, suspended instances due to a message problem are not resumable, and the message itself must be fixed and resubmitted to the BizTalk Server system.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1215">Suspended queue (訊息擱置佇列)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1215">Suspended queue</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1216">包含處理時碰到錯誤或失敗之工作項目的佇列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1216">A queue that contains work items for which an error or failure was encountered during processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1217">訊息擱置佇列會儲存訊息直到修正和重新處理或是刪除後為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1217">A suspended queue stores the messages until they can be corrected and reprocessed, or deleted.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1243">tooltip (工具提示)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1243">tooltip</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1244">當您將滑鼠指標移到項目上的時候，可提供簡短即時線上說明的小型快顯視窗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1244">A little pop-up window that provides brief context-sensitive help when you move the mouse pointer over the item.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1249">Tracking Analysis database (追蹤分析資料庫)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1249">Tracking Analysis database</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1250">相關聯 MessageBox 群組的追蹤分析 (OLAP) 資料庫的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1250">The name of the tracking analysis (OLAP) database for the associated MessageBox group.</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1257">Tracking Options view (追蹤選項檢視)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1257">Tracking Options view</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1258">[ 群組中樞] 頁面上可定義追蹤選項的一種檢視 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1258">A view on the Group Hub page that defines the tracking options.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1259">tracking profile (追蹤設定檔)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1259">tracking profile</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1260">定義商務相關程序且包含特定協調流程與活動定義之間對應的一組特性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1260">A set of characteristics that define a business-related process and contains the mapping between a specific orchestration and activity definition.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1261">追蹤設定檔的副檔名為 .btt。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1261">A tracking profile is a file with a .btt extension.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1262">Tracking Profile Editor (追蹤設定檔編輯器)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1262">Tracking Profile Editor</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1263">圖形使用者介面工具，用來定義其商務程序有興趣的部分以及有興趣的商務內容資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1263">A graphical user-interface tool used to define the interesting parts of their business process as well as interesting business payload data.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1264">交易夥伴</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1264">trading partner</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1265">與貴組織交換電子資料的外部組織或內部組織。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1265">An external or internal organization with which your organization exchanges electronic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1266">例如，交易夥伴可能是供應商、客戶或內部部門。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1266">For example, a trading partner could be a supplier, a customer, or an internal department.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1267">交易夥伴協議</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1267">trading partner agreement</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1268">兩個交易夥伴之間透過特定 B2B 通訊協定交易訊息時所採用的決定性與繫結性協議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1268">A definitive and binding agreement between two trading partners for transacting messages over a specific business-to-business protocol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1269">交易夥伴協議會將在雙方合作對象所屬商務設定檔中共同的雙向訊息處理屬性收集在一起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1269">A trading partner agreement brings together common bi-directional message processing properties from specific business profiles of both partners.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1270">這完整收集了兩個交易夥伴之間進行商務交易時受制於的所有層面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1270">It is a comprehensive collection of all aspects governing the business transaction between the two trading partners.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1271">交易夥伴協議通常是透過設定每個合作夥伴的設定檔而產生，並可讓人自訂和覆寫必要設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1271">The trading partner agreement is typically derived from the profiles of each partner, with the ability to customize and override the required settings.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1272">trading partner management (交易夥伴管理)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1272">trading partner management</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1273">管理及儲存夥伴、其業務和 B2B 關係/協議之相關資訊的動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1273">The act of managing and storing information about partners, their business, and business-to-business relationships/agreements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1274">增強的交易夥伴管理 (TPM) 方案可以更直覺地反映出商務實體與關係，而讓組織能夠更妥善地管理與交易夥伴的商務合作關係。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1274">The enhanced trading partner management (TPM) solution more intuitively reflects the business entities and relationships, thereby enabling organizations to better manage business partnerships with trading partners.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1275">trading party (交易合作對象)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1275">trading party</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1276">位於交易夥伴管理 (TPM) 方案根層級的實體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1276">An entity that is at the root level of a trading partner management (TPM) solution.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1277">進行中商務關係中的每個參與組織，以及執行 BizTalk Server 並與其他合作對象往來傳送訊息的任何單一商務實體，都屬於交易合作對象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1277">Each participating organization in an ongoing business relationship, and any single business entity that is running BizTalk Server and sending or receiving messages to or from any other party, is a trading party.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1278">transactional messaging (交易式傳訊)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1278">transactional messaging</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1279">依序一次傳送的訊息流，藉由同步化和協調群組中多個 BizTalk 訊息佇列配接器執行個體來完成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1279">A stream of messages sent in order exactly once, achieved by synchronizing and coordinating multiple BizTalk message queuing adapter instances in a group.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1280">轉換圖形</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1280">Transform shape</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1281">協調流程中的圖形，用來從一個訊息移動資料到另一個訊息，然後使用 XSLT 對應將它轉換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1281">A shape in an orchestration that is used to move data from one message into another message, and have it transformed using an XSLT map.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1282">轉換</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1282">transformation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1283">將符合一個結構描述的 XML 文件轉換到符合另一個結構描述的 XML 文件的程序，通常在處理過程中會變更文件結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1283">The process of converting an XML document that conforms to one schema into an XML document that conforms to another schema, often changing the document structure in the process.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1284">translation (轉譯)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1284">translation</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1285">將 XML 文件轉換成原生 (非 XML) 格式、或反之亦然的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1285">The process of converting an XML document into native (non-XML) format, or vice versa.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1286">transport agreement (傳輸協議)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1286">transport agreement</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1287">指兩個交易夥伴的商務設定檔之間，規定要使用特定傳輸通訊協定 (AS2) 來交換訊息的協議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1287">An agreement between the business profiles of two trading partners to use a specific transport protocol (AS2) while exchanging messages.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1288">Transport Layer Security (傳輸層安全性)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1288">Transport Layer Security</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1289">一種通訊協定，可提供透過網路進行通訊的兩個應用程式之間的通訊私密性與安全性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1289">A protocol that provides communications privacy and security between two applications communicating over a network.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1290">TLS 會將通訊加密，並可讓用戶端驗證伺服器以及 (選擇性) 讓伺服器驗證用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1290">TLS encrypts communications and enables clients to authenticate servers and, optionally, servers to authenticate clients.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1291">TLS 是比較安全的安全通訊端層 (SSL) 通訊協定版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1291">TLS is a more secure version of the Secure Sockets Layer (SSL) protocol.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1292">transport protocol (傳輸通訊協定)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1292">transport protocol</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1293">一種通訊協定，可控管用於在兩個夥伴之間往返傳送訊息的傳輸通道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1293">A protocol that governs the transport channel used for sending messages back and forth between two partners.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1294">在交易夥伴管理 (TPM) 方面，則僅支援 AS2 通訊協定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1294">With respect to trading partner management (TPM), only the AS2 protocol is supported.</span></span>|  
  
## <a name="u"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-1295">U</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1295">U</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1296">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1296">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1297">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1297">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1298">undeploy (解除部署)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1298">undeploy</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1299">從 BizTalk Server 資料庫和管理主控台刪除 BizTalk 應用程式，並從任何已安裝的電腦上移除應用程式的程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1299">The process of deleting a BizTalk application from the BizTalk Server databases and Administration Console, as well as removing the application from any computers on which it was installed.</span></span>|

## <a name="w"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-1321">W</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1321">W</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1322">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1322">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1323">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1323">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1324">Web 服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1324">Web services</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1325">應用程式邏輯單元，對其他應用程式提供資料和服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1325">A unit of application logic providing data and services to other applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1326">應用程式使用標準 Web 通訊協定和資料格式 (如 HTTP、XML 和 SOAP) 存取 XML Web 服務，與每個 XML Web 服務實作的方式無關。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1326">Applications access XML Web services using standard Web protocols and data formats such as HTTP, XML, and SOAP, independent of how each XML Web service is implemented.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1327">XML Web 服務結合元件基礎開發和 Web 的最佳層面，是 .NET 程式開發模型的基石。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1327">XML Web services combine the best aspects of component-based development and the Web, and are a cornerstone of the Microsoft .NET programming model.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1328">Web Services Description Language (WSDL) (Web 服務描述語言)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1328">Web Services Description Language (WSDL)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1329">一種 XML 格式的語言，可將 Web 服務描述為交換訊息的端點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1329">An XML-formatted language that describes Web services as endpoints for exchanging messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1330">可以將它擴充，以允許描述端點和其訊息，而不論訊息格式和網路通訊協定為何。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1330">It is extensible to allow for the description of endpoints and their messages regardless of the message format and network protocol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1331">這是「通用描述、探索與整合」(UDDI) 所使用的語言 (UDDI 是一種以 Web 為基礎的商務名錄)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1331">It is the language used by Universal Description, Discovery, and Integration (UDDI), which is a Web-based business directory.</span></span>|

## <a name="x"></a><span data-ttu-id="cc989-1340">X</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1340">X</span></span>  
  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1341">詞彙</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1341">Term</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1342">定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1342">Definition</span></span>|  
|----------|----------------|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1343">X.509 certificate (X.509 憑證)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1343">X.509 certificate</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1344">Windows 憑證程序所採用的標準憑證格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1344">The standard certificate format used by Windows certificate-based processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1345">X.509 憑證包含憑證核發對象的個人或實體的公開金鑰及相關資訊、憑證的相關資訊，可能還有核發憑證的憑證授權單位 (CA) 的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1345">An X.509 certificate includes the public key and information about the person or entity to whom the certificate is issued, information about the certificate, plus optional information about the certification authority (CA) issuing the certificate.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1346">XDR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1346">XDR</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1347">請參閱 XML-Data Reduced。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1347">See XML-Data Reduced.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1348">XML Schema definition language (XSD) (XML 結構描述定義語言)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1348">XML Schema definition language (XSD)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1349">結構描述語言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1349">A schema language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1350">XML 結構描述所定義的項目、屬性和資料類型符合「全球資訊網協會 (W3C) XML 結構描述 Part 1：XML 結構描述定義語言的結構推薦」標準。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1350">An XML Schema defines the elements, attributes, and data types that conform to the World Wide Web Consortium (W3C) XML Schema Part 1: Structures Recommendation for the XML Schema Definition Language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1351">「W3C XML 結構描述 Part 2：資料類型推薦」則針對定義 XML 結構描述中所使用的資料類型提供建議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1351">The W3C XML Schema Part 2: Datatypes Recommendation is the recommendation for defining data types used in XML schemas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1352">XML 結構描述定義語言讓您定義 XML 訊息的結構和資料類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1352">The XML Schema definition language enables you to define the structure and data types for XML messages.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1353">XML-Data Reduced (XDR)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1353">XML-Data Reduced (XDR)</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1354">可以描述 XML 文件結構的數種方式之一。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1354">One of several ways in which the structure of an XML document can be described.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1355">BizTalk Server 可以開啟使用 XDR 所描述的結構描述，但在處理過程中會將其轉換成 XML 結構描述定義語言 (XSD)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1355">BizTalk Server can open a schema described using XDR, but converts it to XML Schema definition language (XSD) in the process.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1356">XPath</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1356">XPath</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1357">用來巡覽 XML 文件階層結構的完整語言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1357">A comprehensive language used for navigating through the hierarchy of an XML document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1358">XPath 運算式可以包含 XML 項目和屬性資訊，選取符合特定準則的資料，並在擷取的資料上執行比較。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1358">XPath expressions can contain XML element and attribute information, select data that matches specific criteria, and perform comparisons on the data retrieved.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="cc989-1359">也稱為節點路徑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1359">Also called a node path.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1360">XSD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1360">XSD</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1361">請參閱 XML Schema Definition language (XML 結構描述定義語言)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1361">See XML Schema Definition language.</span></span>|  
|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1362">XSLT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1362">XSLT</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="cc989-1363">請參閱 Extensible Stylesheet Language Transformations (可延伸樣式表語言轉換)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="cc989-1363">See Extensible Stylesheet Language Transformations.</span></span>|
